# Big & Dandy Cocaine Thread

****Cocaine Mega Thread and FAQ**
**


This FAQ is going to cover the basic, most commonly asked questions on BL. More detailed information can be found in the threads linked below.


**My dealer told me my coke is pure. Is it?**


No. If you are in any country outside of South America, there is a 100% chance your cocaine is not going to be pure. Even if you are in South America, unless you are extracting the cocaine yourself, there is still a very high chance that your cocaine is not pure either. Coke is cut even before it leaves the country in which it was produced. Once it makes it to it's destination country, you can pretty much assume with great certainty that it is cut every time it gets in the hands of each dealer or distributor in line before it gets to your dealer. Once it gets to him, he will most likely cut it one last time before he sells it to you. Average purity of cocaine in quantities under 10 grams was 62%. Even if you did wind up with cocaine that pure, you are one the lucky ones.


**If my coke is not pure, what is in it?**


This is probably the most commonly asked question. The problem with this is, no one is going to be able to tell you. The only way to find out is to have some sort of test ran on it. Whether it be with a GC/MS, some Marquis or Reagent testing, I have no idea, but the fact is, we will not be able to tell you from 1,000 miles away over the internet.


However, there are a couple cuts that have been showing up more frequently, and those are amphetamines. The best way to know if you have amphetamines is to pay attention to how the cocaine is affecting you. Cocaine is not the energetic, bouncing off the walls drug that everyone tends to make it out to be. If you are over-energetic, cannot sit still, have feelings of isolation or wanting to be left alone, excessive talking, or you have the shakes, those are all signs of amphetamines.


**If those effects are from amphetamines, what is good coke supposed to feel like?**


As Erowid.org describes it:


> Varies with dose and the tolerance of the user. Increases alertness, wakefulness, elevates the mood, mild to high degree of euphoria, increases athletic performance, decreases fatigue, clearer thinking, increases concentration, increases energy, increased irritability, insomnia, restlessness.
> 		
> Click to expand...


The effects of coke are more relaxing than people assume. It's a mild energy that it provides. Good coke will not make you feel an urge to get up and move around all night. You will feel perfectly content with lying in bed watching a movie, or sitting around talking with a group of friends. It causes euphoria, and puts you in a good state of mind. It does not make you want to be alone and does not make you talk incessantly without finishing one coherent sentence. It provides clarity, so it should actually be a lot easier to convey your thoughts with words.


Do not be fooled by the amphetamine ridden garbage circulating all over the world now. If you like that kind of thing, go ahead and get it, but you're not doing real cocaine when you are doing it. You're doing amphetamines.


**How much coke do I need for a fun night?**


It depends. Are you doing it alone? If not, how many people are you doing it with? How experienced with cocaine are you and your friends?


There are many variables that make this question almost impossible to answer. The best advice anyone would be able to give you is to just spend as much money as you are willing to spend, and if it turns out you bought more than you need, just save it for another time. There is never anything wrong with buying too much, but it would really suck if you bought too little.


As an estimate, for non tolerant users of cocaine, get about a half gram of cocaine per person.


**How much cocaine should I do?**


If you're asking this question, it's obvious you are inexperienced with cocaine. For someone new to the drug, it's suggested to take a normal sized match stick, cut it in half, and do a line of cocaine that is the same size as that matchstick.


To be honest, it's going to be very hard to OD off one line of cocaine. As long as you aren’t doing a line that’s 5 inches long, you'll be fine. You could get away with doing a line up 1.5 or 2 inches long (skinny line, not fat) for your first time and be perfectly OK, but it's always best to start small, that’s why you should go with the matchstick idea.


One thing to remember with any drug is “you can always do more, but you can never do less.”


**What are good drugs to mix with cocaine?**


The answer to this question is highly subjective. It depends on what you like. A few things that are commonly take along side cocaine are benzodiazepines, marijuana, and opiates. Remember, when mixing cocaine with any drug, always do a little bit less than you would normally do of each drug. Also, make sure you are experienced with both drugs on their own before mixing them.


The easier question to answer is what NOT to mix with cocaine. There are two obvious answers. One, MDMA. Two, alcohol. Mixing cocaine with MDMA will totally negate the effects of the MDMA. Some people report that cocaine on the comedown of an MDMA high is good. At this point in the high, the desired effects of MDMA have worn off, so there is no longer any worry of negating the effects. The problem is, you won’t feel the typical euphoria from the cocaine. It will give you energy and positive mood lift, but the euphoria is greatly diminished.


Mixing alcohol with cocaine is dangerous because of the chemical cocaethylene. It's a chemical that is highly toxic to the liver. Despite this, drinking alcohol while consuming cocaine is a very popular practice amongst cocaine users, mostly due to them being uninformed of the dangers.


**I'm all out of coke and I feel like shit, I can’t sleep, and I have to be at work in 5 hours. What do I do?**


The comedown: everyone’s least favorite part of using cocaine. The good thing is, it's easy to deal with. A good tip for anyone using cocaine who knows they won’t be able to sleep at the end of the night is to make sure you have some sort of depressant drug on hand BEFORE doing the coke. The mad dash to find such drugs at 4am always ends up unsuccessful so make sure you have them before you start blowing lines.


Typical drugs used for the comedown are opiates and benzodiazepines. Good opiates to use include Hydrocodone, Oxycodone, and even Heroin. Good benzos to use would be Alprazolam, Diazepam, Clonazepam, or even Triazolam. There are many others of both opiates and benzos. These are just examples. If you have a favorite opiate or benzo, you can just use that instead.


Marijuana can be a decent choice, but it can also be a really bad choice. It's common for inexperienced users to really freak out from smoking pot while on coke. So, if you're going to use pot, be sure you'll be able to handle it.

1) Is it going to kill me?

2) Is it going to kill me if I work out with it?

3) Is it going to kill me if I use it a couple of times a week?

4) Does the acetone wash treatment work?

5) Is it an effective study drug

Hey DangerChamber


I think it depends how much you take. It'll increase your heart rate so if you have a congenital heart defect it could place enough load to trigger a heart attack, which could be fatal. If you're already pretty fit you should be fine.


From your questions it seems like you've never used it before but you're thinking about taking it regularly to help with studying and exercise. I don't think that's a good idea at all. 


The more you use it the more likely you are to develop a dependence on it.


Think of it this way: when you start it may help you study/work out, but the way the brain works means that you will need more to regain that magic you felt at the start. 


Then the coke may become unavailable and studying/exercise will be harder than when you started using - the activities may become totally unrewarding and you may have problems with motivation.


If you really want to try it, use the least amount you can to obtain the desired effects, and try to avoid long-term use.


Maybe I've misread your situation - what are your thoughts?

<!-- POST END: id=8152596 -->

1. It *probably* won't kill you, but it could if you were extremely irresponsible.


2. Again, the potential's there. Just do everything in moderation and you'll be alright.


3. You don't want a cocaine dependency, and that's all that will come of it.


4. If you've never done coke I wouldn't worry about acetone washing anything just yet.


5. No, it most likely will not help you study. As soon as your high you'll feel jacked and be too distracted with other things. Then when you come down you won't want to do your work and you'll be probably be trying to redose. And the cycle continues until you're out of coke/money...

people say, when you get good coke, you'll know.  I bought some coke and got kinda ripped off one line, but i'm very new to experimenting with cocaine, and i don't know fi the high i feel is intense or not, it doesn't feel intense, but i don't know if its strong compared to the good stuff.  apparently its 70% pure,  Last time i bought of this connect it was cut way to much and burned my nose a lot. and i told him i was not pleased with it, he said don't worry next time it will be better promise, and it is  it didn't burn my nose and i got a lot more high.  but i still don't know if he is just cutting it with something different so it doesn't burn my nose, or is he gave a legit count this time


so my question is.

Q: How do i know if my coke im doing is strong?

I would be flabbergasted if your product was actually 70% pure Cocaine.  I would be extremely surprised/impressed/jealous if it was even 40-50% pure.  There is a water test you can perform to estimate actual Coca content vs. cuts.  Do a search and you will find how to do it.

<!-- POST START: id=8249705 num=29 author=xikito author_id=151845 date=2010-04-03T03:08:43+0100 -->
### Post #29

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 8249705 |
| Author | xikito |
| Author ID | 151845 |
| Date | Apr 3, 2010 at 3:08 AM |
| Page | 2 |

Here is a good question, how to know the coke your snorting is good quality?


I've heard things like "no taste at all is better" and "petrol like smell and flavour" means the shit is better quality... the truth is, with amphetamines in the mix is very hard to know how good coke is (some feelings mix together and is difficult do discern to a novice user).


I've been a novice user for some time now (I only snort around twice a year, for 4 years now), and have been getting my white in different places every time and they are never ever the same!


My experience tells me:

- If you can feel a very acid/burning taste or feeling after you snort, it is because it is cut with something that is causing that reaction (not good!).

- No taste and odour means more tremors/shackiness and bigger comedown; which leads me to believe it has been cut with amphetamines (not good!).

- Soft acid taste with strong petrol smell: very good hights with lesser comedowns (still a major pain in my ass! coke comedowns are the worse I've felt!). The best I've personally tried.

<!-- POST END: id=8249705 -->

> LSDMDMA&8168748 said:
> 			
> 		
> 
> 
> 			yep. Stims are that way, speed does it to me. More of mix of anger and sadness afterwards, though
> 		
> Click to expand...
> — LSDMDMA&8168748 said:


After doing adderall for about 2 and a half weeks I agree.  I couldn't pinpoint it at first, I thought it was just me being emo, but that feeling of despair must definitely be due to the amphetamines.


Good read on cocaine purity tests for the ignorant (me).  I didn't know about this so sorry if this is common knowledge for everyone else


[http://books.google.com/books?id=OT...esnum=10&ved=0CCsQ6AEwCQ#v=onepage&q=&f=false](https://books.google.com/books?id=OTAlolM3XlwC&pg=PA37&lpg=PA37&dq=stannous+chloride+cocaine&source=bl&ots=AhuFo_bMK9&sig=6Nob35HbOrprYRvRQC5NjWzcUqY&hl=en&ei=vLS2S4itFIS-8wTe39nqAw&sa=X&oi=book_result&ct=result&resnum=10&ved=0CCsQ6AEwCQ#v=onepage&q=&f=false)


Page 37 is particularly interesting.  To sum it up


- Most common cuts do not dissolve in pure methanol, but cocaine does (methamphetamine does as well, don't know about the other amps)

- Cocaine burns clear, while sugar cuts will dirty the smoke, amphetamines will pop

- The use of stannus chloride.  All -caine cuts dissolve, while cocaine does not.  Readily available on amazon, I believe.

- Water test.  Cocaine dissolves almost instantly while the other cuts will more slowly.

- True cocaine has a shiny glittery appearance, unique to the appearance of most cutting agents.

**Crack vs Powder: crack fails**


I promised myself since the first time I stole my dad's vodka that I would never smoke crack, well I broke that promise. I figured what the hell? It's worth tryin once right? Nooooooooo. Not at all.  I'm a big fan of the powder though.


The chick I was doing it with said it was good and she seemed quite jacked from it. I wanted a bellringer or whatever, just to experience it. I know other powder users who have told me its worth trying once just for that. I wasn't aware there was a such a fine tuned technique to smoking crack properly, she tried to show me but I think I kept fucking it up. Anyways all I know is I wasted $50 that would have been much better spent on some powder or weed. Either would have lasted more than 20 minutes.


I got some thick white hits upon exhalation, we were smokin through a stem. It tasted like a woobanger rolled with nasty resin instead of weed.


I'm still after that bellringer, so any tips if I ever decide to try this again? It would have to be someone else's gear cuz theres no way I'm wasting any of my powder that way. I just hope I never cross the other two lines I forbid myself to cross...needles and meth.

<!-- POST END: id=8312267 -->

Crack is wack seriously I ended up in rehab at 15 for crack/powder cocaine and iv morphine/oxycodone addiction. 


If you want a "bellringer" like someone mentioned before just fucking shoot it. Make sure you can shoot the coke though BE CAREFUL. There was an epidemic of blindness when I got out of rehab from people shooting coke that was cut bad.  


Also since this is a megathread I have a question about the coke culture I would like to ask and see if anyone agrees with me.


Q: After the recent emergence of "cocaine rap" which I have nothing against, at all. And I know rappers have always rapped about it but recently it has been popularized again. I thkn this has lead to the influx of dirty coke going around. Everyone wants to be a coke slingin' scarface and sell shit they have no idea about. Every little hustler out there will sell you white shit in a bag thinking they are hustlin when in reality they are pushing customers away. I truly believe its a conspiracy that this influx of coke rap has caused more "drug naive" dealers to sell shit product because the demand will never cease.

> Crack is wack
> 		
> Click to expand...


Agreed.


> If you want a "bellringer" like someone mentioned before just fucking shoot it. Make sure you can shoot the coke though BE CAREFUL. There was an epidemic of blindness when I got out of rehab from people shooting coke that was cut bad.
> 		
> Click to expand...


Fuck that no needles for me, and blindness doesn't seem worth it for a bellringer. Maybe I'll never experience one, from my once experience with crack I doubt I'm missing much anyway. Snorting is so much better, and way more social.


Coke/rack rapping? ...IDK since I listen to mostly punk and classic rock. But there is a ALOT of shitty coke out there. The overall quality of blow seems worse than it was when I was into it 5 or so years ago.


> Is it true that if you do it more than once over the course of 2 nights your going to be addicted ?
> 		
> Click to expand...


No. But if you do it once there's a good chance you will like it, which is already a step towards addiction.  But after my experiences with opiates I'm not sure true cocaine addiction even exists. Be careful though.


> Do you think it would be safe to do it all in one night ?
> 		
> Click to expand...


Safe or not...there's a rule about cocaine. Whatever you buy there's a decent chance it will all be gone by the morning. Start slow.


> Is there anything other than benzo's and opiates to help with the comedown ? (legal stuff)
> 		
> Click to expand...


Not exactly legal but some dank will kill the jones and maybe allow you to sleep. Not sure why you care if it's legal since coke is anything but. Nothing beats weed + xanax though.


> How long will the comedown last, because i've done MDMA before and I could handle the comedown with ease. Is the comedown for coke worse than MDMA ?
> 		
> Click to expand...


Depends mostly on the quality of the blow, and how much you do. If it's decent yak the up/down should be fairly smooth, but again weed will help smooth it out.


> Is a party a good scene to be at while we are on it ?
> 		
> Click to expand...


Maybe, but even though you think you can act sober on coke other people will notice. They may even want some.


All in all, start slow, be safe, and have fun. Don't get busted! ![=D](https://bluelight.org/xf/BL_Images/Orig_Emoji/biggrin.gif)

New amesome thingy- READ ME

So Lots of pEople around here love coke.  Apparently quality has gone up lots the past year and wasn't total shit or anything like that before the quality went up(new dealer here).  I tried a few times(snorting), and it didn't work, ever, giving me nose bleeds.  This was from the same bag, equal or bigger than other peoles lines who would be loving it, and nothing but some jitters for me.


Waited a few months, then earlier today snorted 170mg(so bigger than normal line of this, "normal" seems to be about 100mg), right away nose bleeds(that nostril, ended up not being too bad though, will clean nostril sooN).

No feeling 5 minutes later


6-10 minutes later, put 250-300mg under my tongue and 100mg on my gums(THIS wasn't as good as the snorted line earlier BTW, I was given it from a friend who owed me money, he said it wasn't quite as good and told me that I'd be smart enough to figure out how to get it in me without my nose or the ROAs not used around here(nobody smokes crack or IVs that I know)), let rest about 6 minutes, till no chunks/anything is left, just a thick saliva with wierd texture, let sit longer(held all the thick mouth wierdo stuff on gums for a few minutes).


Spit that into shot glass, then filled it with 21% alc, drank, filled again most of way and drank.

30 seconds later I get all jittery than get hit by that nice coke feeling I hadn't truely had before, with music sounding better and being all hyper and such.


So I finally get it, and thought I'd let people know this way does work(the line I(stupidly) snorted did not contribute IMO, I'd tried this coke before, thought I'd try again today hoping for no nose bleed or something, nothing from it).  From the people around me, I am better off than they are from 200mg lines.


So there you go.  Soon I'll try it again, ONLY under my tongue(sublingually is the word I've found here for that), only 200mg, then spit into like 60% alc, take 1 or 2 shots and see how it goes.

 Will update when I'm all crashy, it's lasted 30ish minutes now.  Possibly the crash will be better than people get snorting(probably just being hopefull).  May also help that I'm not re dosing.


ADDING EDIT: Anywhere I should post this?  I tried looking up many oral cocaine things on BL and didn't find much helpful info.

BTW, been good 45ish minutes now, is wearing off a bit but no bad feeling(I remember it taking like 2 hours to feel bad though, my friends just left for a few minutes so I've got nobody to ask).  Same heart beat as 15 minutes ago.

> what could create dopamine levels
> 		
> Click to expand...
Dopamine precursors of course ![;)](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/8.0/png/unicode/64/1f609.png)

Phenylalanine and Tyrosine come to mind.

Although in all honestly, all you really should need is a good night's sleep, some excersize, and a decent meal.  A short break from drugs couldn't hurt either ![;)](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/8.0/png/unicode/64/1f609.png)


> i did the benadryll once for an ex comedown it put me to sleep but i couldnt pee for weeks **maybe an allergic reaction** perhaps my bladder elt swollen for like a month
> 		
> Click to expand...
Unlikely, as diphenhydramine(benadryl) is a histamine antagonist.

<!-- POST START: id=8334779 num=68 author=JoshuaV author_id=113237 date=2010-04-29T14:45:40+0100 -->
### Post #68

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 8334779 |
| Author | JoshuaV |
| Author ID | 113237 |
| Date | Apr 29, 2010 at 2:45 PM |
| Page | 4 |

I think 0.3g is enough, if you have decent quality supplies and you've no tolerance. I usually buy a .5 for myself and it lasts me the whole night, easy.


Then again I'm not much into coke, and I prefer milder doses to heavy doses (probably due to my stuff not being pure). I like doing small bumps frequently rather than long lines every hour. 


Also if you're coke-naive, you're better to start with a small bump to see how it makes you feel. You don't want to do a big line and have it make you all jittery and uncomfortable. I once eyeballed an amount of coke to add to my coffee in the morning, taking into account an assumed BA of 2:1 (meaning I put twice as much in to drink as I would have snorted). The end result was me getting reaaaally nauseous and dizzy, feeling like my heart was going to blow, and having to lie down for an hour. Almost no euphoria or pleasant effects.


EDIT: for your last question, "How should I space them out", you'll have to go by feel. When you feel ready for more, do more. You'll know once you're in the situation.

<!-- POST END: id=8334779 -->

Treatment? I would imagine enforced Abstinence, group therapy, life coaching etc..

I'm not sure if there are any drug based treatments for cocaine addiction if thats what you are getting at..

**iv coke crazy echo**


so i just did what was definitely in the top 3 most reckless things ive done in my drug career. i just eyeball dosed a shot of coke (which i havent done in a good 4 months) and just had the most intense rush ever, never experienced anything like it. i eyeballed cause i was at work and in a hurry, usually it takes about 20sec to feel it but this was instant and it felt like it was mixed with K (but i know it wasnt). the ringing was really strong but everything started echoing like fucing crazy, and this wasnt typical ecoing, every little tiny noise had this crazy fuckin echo. i honesty thought there HAD to be someone else in the bathroom making the noise, but it was empty.  cleaned everything as fast as possible and flushed the rig cause i thought i was gonna have a stroke and i didnt want it to look suspicious if someone found me unconscious. could i have gotten a stroke what are the chances of that?

Acetone bath won't remove all cuts/impurities, especially the most widely used one: levamisole. Try rocking it up and then reconverting to HCL. That will help but won't remove the Levami. ![:\](https://bluelight.org/xf/BL_Images/Orig_Emoji/wrygrin.gif)

My first time doing coke was filthyyyyyy. (filthy = slang for cool)


Me and my friends had talked about doing coke, but hadnt tried it yet.


Summer before my senior year of high school I go to Whistler, Canada to stay at my condo with my family. I wanted to bring a friend but they all had football so I went alone, super bummed.

Turns out the weekend we were there was this huge mt. biking competition so the village was like a huge party all weekend. Awsome!


I ran into a girl from school. So we hungout. At night some kid came up to us looking for yayo. I was like "sorry dude cant help you" but then I decided to help him look for some.

We were just about to give up when I found some.

I got a half gram **snip** but I dont care ahaha I have money.

Me and her each did half (so .25 each) and within like ... 5-10 minutes im just NUMB.

I keep saying "OMG Im SOO high right now" 


Ive done coke 5-7 times since never come close to that high.

> My dealer told me my coke is pure. Is it?
> 
> 
> 
> No. If you are in any country outside of South America, there is a 100% chance your cocaine is not going to be pure. Even if you are in South America, unless you are extracting the cocaine yourself, there is still a very high chance that your cocaine is not pure either.
> 		
> Click to expand...


%100 true! I live in South America and as me and my friends always talk about, the pure coke leaves SA and gets cut x10 in europe or u.s.a, either way i know the coke we get is obviously more pure than the coke in u.s.a or europe but no way is it %100 pure, i'd say %40-50 with a good connection, could be higher and could be lower but no way is it pure and i live in one of the countrys that produce most cocaine in the world. In Peru if you want %95 pure cocaine its out there but you have to buy a kilo and know the right people and your everyday drug user wont buy that much, especially knowing the time jail time it would land you and here $1200-1500 is allot of money, what allot of people make working hard in one year.

[QUOTE

The effects of coke are more relaxing than people assume. It's a mild energy that it provides. Good coke will not make you feel an urge to get up and move around all night. You will feel perfectly content with lying in bed watching a movie, or sitting around talking with a group of friends. It causes euphoria, and puts you in a good state of mind. It does not make you want to be alone and does not make you talk incessantly without finishing one coherent sentence. It provides clarity, so it should actually be a lot easier to convey your thoughts with words.

------------ unquote]

Sometimes, i get coke that makes me feel stoned. I get all relaxed, and just wanna sprawl out on the couch and stare into space. It's nice, but if I wanted that effect I could've gotten some good bud.  Other times, I get coke that reeks of ether and burns like paint thinner in my nose. It makes my lips, tongue and mouth numb, my heart beat fast, my stomach flip, and I feel f---in amazing. (the song "invincible" by adelitas way pretty much describes it) I want to listen to hard rock and dance like a stripper, I don't want to be alone, I want people to see me. Sometimes my nose will bleed, and the blood will make my upper lip numb. I want to talk about drugs, think about drugs, and do more drugs when I'm on this kind of coke.  I'm guessing thats the amphetamines talking right now...

Also, I noticed that the day after I do coke, i sometimes take OTC pills with 500 mg acetaminophen and 60 mg of caffiene. I take between 2 and 4 of these over a few hours for headaches. A bit later, I get this trippy, disconnected feeling, like I'm floating. I never knew acetaminophen had "recreational effects", but its pretty cool... Except when I'm sitting in an art class, trying to paint a lemon, and all of a sudden my hand isn't mine. I asked the teacher to take a break, and I wanted to go lay in the grass outside. Any ideas why this happens? It's only when I take the pills the day after doing coke

<!-- POST END: id=9789804 -->

just how bad is a coke binge? I've hit about 4 or 5 rails today total but all spaced about 2 hours apart, and well as anyone knows after a night of doing coke (or day in this case) you probably aren't going to sleep anytime soon without the aid of benzos or seroquel or whatever, but I don't have those, I only have like .5 of pot and some clonidine that actually put me in a worse state instead of making me pass out unless combined with other OTC sleep aids which I also currently don't have, I'm well aware it was probably a stupid idea to do coke without benzos or whatever on hand but I did anyways, so now I'm wondering if it would be a bad idea to wait to sleep til tonight and would it be an even worse idea to do a few more rails through the day? if so, why? what am I risking? I appreciate the response in advance.

Wow I just got the strongest coke of my life from a delivery service in Brooklyn. Man do they have their shit on lock. The receptionist takes the order after verifying your name, she then uses her computer to determine where her delivery drivers are by using that sprint/nextel service for business owners who have a fleet and want to be able to walkie talki bleep each other as well as locate via GPS. She sends whoever is closest onto the next delivery. IMO its a pretty legit delivery service they got goin on there. On top of that, if a runner gets arrested they pay for counsel in return for not ratting.


The coke is nice fluffy coke that is almost like oily in texture.. ideally you would use a razor blade to cut it up. I have been getting dubs from Paterson which are soft/rocks/etc.. and I consider it to be 'good.' Well this stuff BLEW the ptown coke out of the water. 70mg hit me like a freight train and trumped the 200mg shots I have been doing by FAR. I got a orgasmic bellringer and a rush that I can only hope is what life feels like in heaven. It was just pure total bliss multiplied by 1,000,000.


Another cool, thing is that literally as soon as water hits the coke it turns to a 100% completely clear mixture./ I did nto even have to do a single stir (atleast not for the coke, for the dope I did).  Man I can't imagine what would have happened if I did a 200mg shot without testing it. I got scared that the 70mg shot was putting me 6' under but I leveled off nicely.

The last day I used cocaine was july 23rd, that means I'm 7 weeks and 5 days completely sober from cocaine ![:)](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/8.0/png/unicode/64/1f642.png) Monday will mark 2 months, and other than some occasional use of the RC ethylphenidate, and with it etizolam, I'm completely clean of any other hard drugs ![:)](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/8.0/png/unicode/64/1f642.png) Feels great to not be scrumabing together enough money every week to at least buy a gram of blow, and EPH has worked great as a "methadone-esque" solution to my cravings, just as methadone is used for heroin withdrawal.  This is great, a gram of EPH lasts me weeks without issue, is more potent, is far less impulsive IMO as far as re-dosing goes, and costs a fourth of the price.  Haven't had a cocaine craving in weeks either, EPH really helped in that category as well.  I can still see its addictive properties though, so this definitely isn't a permanent solution and I plan on dropping EPH all together soon as well.

<!-- POST END: id=10905403 -->

<!-- POST START: id=10905443 num=141 author=pbuilder author_id=214743 date=2012-09-16T04:56:43+0100 -->
### Post #141

> [Zoeylynn said:](https://www.bluelight.org/community/goto/post?id=10905410)
> 
> 
> 
> 			^ congratulations Pbuilder!! 
> 
> Click to expand...
> — Zoeylynn said:


Thanks ![:)](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/8.0/png/unicode/64/1f642.png)  Prior to this 7 weeks, 5 days clean (which I actually only just calculated right now, because cocaine was so far off my mind I wasn't even counting sober days anymore ^-^), the most I'd went clean was 15 days.  During a period from october 2011 to july 2012, I was using at least once a week if not more (other than a single 15 days clean I managed to do once, but than the following weekend quickly gave into the craving and phoned a dealer), and at the very least a half gram in a night, but at the worst parts over a ball in a weekend or even close to in a single night.  


Later in that habitual usage the comedowns got worse and worse, and the high I quickly had fallen in love with become more scarce, and every single time while coming down I would say to myself, this feeling sure as fuck ain't worth it, this is the last damn time ever.  And for a day or two after I would feel the same, still have that horrible come-down anxiety-ridden feeling in my mind and be happy with never doing coke again, but by day 3 or 4 I would forget the negatives and just remember the euphoria, causing me to use again the following weekend, or even sooner.


Thank god I finally had the courage one morning after a 8-ball binge in a night, to take my phone and delete all my dealers, as well as everyone that would even have their numbers.  Same goes for any connections through facebook.


That is what truly helped the most, by having no availability to the drug by placing a quick simple text, it helped tremendously to stop using.  I did try a few times to get dealers numbers through friends of friends but thankfully they never came through, and I haven't even attempted any purchase of the drug in like 6 weeks.


And even worse, just before I quit usage of cocaine I virtually never even snorted it anymore, but rather either did "foilies" where I added a bit of water with half and half coke/baking soda on foil and smeared it equally, and then smoked it, or I cooked it in a spoon and then smoked it off foil as well via chasing, cause where I live actual "glass roses" that are used as crack pipes aren't around in every store. (aren't around at all actually, never seen one). Looking back, I never ever though I'd smoke "crack", or technically ghetto foil freebase, but I so easily in that mind-set justified smoking it that way for the rush, thinking it was no big deal lol... Blocking out the fact that I was literally becoming a crack head.

Sadly almost 2 weeks ago on saturday september the 29th I relapsed and did two and a half lines of blow supplied by a friend.  I was so drunk I barely remember the usage, still remember that beautiful cocaine smell though.  But the following weekend I did MDMA and while rolling I was watching people at my house do blow and thinking god damn thank god I quit that shit, in my head I was just thinking "why the fuck are you guys doing nothing but talking over each other every 10 seconds in a conversation and talking shit to yourselfs even though your friends lol.  Chirping for fun once in a while is one thing, but every convo had everyone just talking shit every other line lol.  This interpretation was likely caused by the fact I was rolling tits on mdma that I think had a fair amount of MDA in it because I was tripping a bit too.


Anyways, so I had that small cocaine relapse 12 days ago, and before that I hadn't used for almost 10 weeks.  Either way, It ain't a big deal and it has already been 12 days since that small relapse and I'm not fiending at all.  When I had formed a small habit I couldn't help but use every weekend, so even just using one more time and then not using for almost 2 weeks again shows I have made serious progress.  Deleting my dealers and any sources at all helped a great amount though.  If I really tried I'm sure I could get a dealers number but I just don't care enough to try and am certain I will go to christmas without using again without problems.  I do plan on using on newyears though, but just as a treat.  New years and my birthday are both 6 months apart so it is perfect, i will only ever use on those two special occasions and the best thing is that the one dealer I do have would only sell it to me on my b-day and new-years because he's a non-greedy friend and a friend of my older bro, so I'm not remotely sweating temptation.  He'd never sell to me on any random weekend, and I know that for a fact because before originally quitting blow he was already just ignoring my txts to pick up, which lead me to another dealer (whom I've deleted now)

<!-- POST END: id=10974791 -->

**My last year**


I'm a massive "coke head". You know, the type that stays clean from any drugs for few weeks then have a massive cocaine binge for a few sleepless nights. (spend around £100-£1000 the more money i spend the more days i`m high) 


Using cocaine makes me feel like i am some *king of the world* type character in the first day of my binge. 

Then there is a huge difference in my high after the first night. Doing the same amount again without sleep (or a few hours sleep) or food and a lack of liquids. 

After the second night, £200 and using all my energy... I feel terrible, but will keep sniffing continuously until ive spent the same amount of money as Greece's Debt. 


My point is, shit cocaine makes you feel like youre in the 3rd day after a few hours. Good cocaine will plessure you for longer, but either way you`ll end up in the same state. SO use coke responsibly, if you complain too much.**![:)](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/8.0/png/unicode/64/1f642.png)![:)](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/8.0/png/unicode/64/1f642.png)**

Just what I pulled up real quick about that substance, since I'd never heard of it before. Stims aren't my thing so I bow to the wisdom of Google lol:


"Benzoylecgonine, also known as ecgonine benzoate, is the main metabolite of cocaine. Produced by hydrolysis, benzoylecgonine can be detected in urine for a minimum of 5 days after usage of cocaine. Heavy usage can lead to detection up to a month after usage, and it can take heavy users up to four months to clean out their system completely"


So yeah, dilute and pray bro, dilute and pray.........

Experience with the EZTest Cocaine test kits?   


EZTest for Cocaine Purity comes back as dark burgundy red -- "Very High Cocaine Content" -- exactly has hoped for.  


Same stuff.  EZTest for Cocaine Cuts comes back as a really dark blackish-yellow.  Any reaction is bad on this one in general but the color it is turning seems to map to either Phenacetine or Ephedrine, I can't really tell which.  


How to interpret these two together?  How does it have high purity but then also says it's cut with something.  


Any input appreciated.

So I got introduced to a new dealer and he is the guy that supplies all the dealers I've gone through since I first started two years ago. I got a gram to start with and when I put it on my car manual the smell was strong. It smelled strongly of paint and just smelling it gave me a rush. I licked the baggie it was in and it numbed my mouth pretty good. When I inspected it I noticed it looked was very shiny like a pearl. I flashed my light on it and it was beautiful. I searched up Fishscale cocaine and what I had in front of me was what came up in my search results. I crushed some up took a bump and instantly felt the effects. No nose burn unlike all the other shit I was getting before. I was already high after a couple bumps which usually would take 5 in each nostril of the shit I was getting before. My nose would always bleed after a session and burn like hell for most of the night. This new stuff not a single drop of blood or burning in my nostrils. I took a picture of it for you to see what I had. [http://image.doc2pdf.net/temp/image.jjpg](http://image.doc2pdf.net/temp/image.jjpg)

<!-- POST START: id=13846879 num=217 author=jawbrah author_id=427648 date=2016-11-09T04:22:38+0000 -->
### Post #217

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 13846879 |
| Author | jawbrah |
| Author ID | 427648 |
| Date | Nov 9, 2016 at 4:22 AM |
| Page | 11 |

Antipsychotics being used in cocaine addiction treatment?


Hello,


So let me give a brief background story, so I was admitted to a hospital because of my "addiction", which wasn't really serious tbh. It all started in late 2014, when I was going to electronic clubs and festivals here in Brazil and using mdma pills mostly, one time a friend had some coke and asked if I wanted some, I was really reluctant because of the stigma cocaine has specially here in Brazil, but used it anyway... long story short I felt a huge increase in confidence (I'm really shy), and felt like a new person, he gave me that g of coke. I actually only used it in special events, and treated it as a "magic" social lubricant wtf haha, it lasted me 2 months... I liked it specially, because it's not so obvious that you're high on coke, as oppsed to mdma that you just use in places where peopel are rolling.


Then I started buying a g every weekend, there was no fun without some yayo, going to bathrooms at bars chopping up lines on my phone at first I was really comfortable with this, then became a little paranoid people would notice. But it was fun doing with friends talking about so many subjects, which I'm not comfortable doing sober, not even alcohol makes me more social, it only makes me tired and sleepy, so in my head it'd help me socialize, I never used alone, always when I needed to be social, a g would last me a long time.


Then one day at work, I was kinda bored went to the bathroom, and decided why not use some to get me through the day, did one line, felt like a new man, started talking to people, was happy working even though tired... you can imagine how it went down, started using to work to socialize and shit.


Fast-forward a few months I decided to use steroids, in hopes it would shift my focus awway from coke, I loved the roids, gained a lot of muscle, strength... but it made me a bit impatient and angry at people.. I was obcessed about getting girls, and this girls I was putting alot of effort into ignored me, and I just lost it broke some shit at home.. and went back to doing cocaine my mom caught me doing some lines, i didn't even care like it was not a big deal.


My mom wanted me to seek treatment in a facility to get clean, at first I thought thats not the case... but then one day I was confused, and went for a visit at this psychiatric ward with my family, and accepted their decision.


It's known to be a psychiatric hospital, but they have drug addiction treatment aswell, what I don't undestand is why they give heavy doses of antipsychotics in the first weeks, like risperdone, haldol IM, quetiapine, Chlorpromazine, Levomepromazine some mood stabilizers too which turned me into a zombie, had some Tardive dyskinesia, could barely eat as my jaw was unresponsive, and they give it to all pacients, for the entire treatment.


I was even strapped to the bed once, because I got irritated by the nurses and staff, they contain you and inject some haldol and Promethazine.


Even after you're released from the hospital they give the drugs to you, but what I don't get is why give this drugs, what relation do they have with cocaine addiction.


I think I developed gyno cause of the prolactin rise, and after I got out I developed some premature ejacualtion, and im depressed too, and i tried some coke and I dont euphoria from it anymore, also i believe that it has some relation to the drugs they gave me. MInd you Im not taking them anymore.


I never heard of rehab centers giving these drugs to apparently treat some addiction decease.


What are you guys opnions on this? could you shed some light on my situation I'm really confused and tired right now

<!-- POST END: id=13846879 -->

Maybe cocaine that was moist from them holding it in their hands..They should not be holding coke in their hands because any sweat will be absorbed into the coke since it is water soluble..high humidity will make coke clumpy and sticky, but letting it dry out in a lower humidity area will let it get back to more powdery, although some people cut the coke with stuff that will make it clumpy or sticky, especially novices to cutting it.

<!-- POST END: id=13886768 -->

I read somewhere it's NOT a good idea to take a beta blocker because of mixed signals to the heart or something but I don't have benzos and this is the next best thing. Paranoria setting in; keep checking that my door is closed and that the cops aren't here. I still have some left that I was SUPPOSED to save for the next day (today, but AFTER sleeping!) The good news is, no nausea, vomiting, or itchiness. Or seeing things that aren't there. <!-- POST START: id=13909150 num=246 author=ShroomySatori author_id=375867 date=2017-01-10T04:44:02+0000 -->
### Post #246

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 13909150 |
| Author | ShroomySatori |
| Author ID | 375867 |
| Date | Jan 10, 2017 at 4:44 AM |
| Page | 13 |

I've always heard this drug is over-rated but I finally got fishscale and in my opinion it's under-rated. 


It makes me feel all chill and smooth and slick, and* really *euphoric.


Not to mention, helps me focus. I can't handle any stimulants like adderall or even coffee as I have a panic disorder but this one is fine. It seems mellow but energizing, with a bit of a crash. 


Also, it keeps my mind off heroin, at least for a while. I haven't used in 12 hours and normally I don't go 4 without a line. If the line is small I can get sick in a few hours so 12 is definitely not normal and has to due with the C use which I'd say has been 50 milligrams total. Also, it helps with the constipation associated with chronic opiate use, just like green tea does. And I can sleep shortly afterwards (like 2 hours). Very functional. I make sure to stay hydrated, take magnesium for the vasoconstriction, and also have several cups of valerian tea to relax a bit (and at some point my daily benzo... haha...)


This is totally under-rated, I always hear people say this is just stomped on shit and I think most of the time it is. I perhaps just got lucky for once, because I don't recall it being very much anything like this. Edgier. More abrasive. It's definitely a little fiendish still since I've kept it going for most of the day. The one major thing for me is that it really drastically reduces H withdrawals. I was not expecting that. I should have needed a hit several hours ago. If I was rich I would totally use this on a regular basis, but the crash is different from being sick which I am very used to by now. The crash feels like it's unhealthy for the body a bit, while opiates certainly are not to any great extent apart from the cycle of addiction which is mainly related to prohibition and inflated costs of these things that should have much less value than they do. It's just an alkaloid from a plant. 


I really need a break from H in terms of tolerances, no intention to quit that is, and haven't been able to manage it after several years the withdrawal has become very relentless so, yeah... not promoting what I'm doing haha but if I'm using C instead of dope and my tolerance to H is lowering while C isn't really my thing, but it's keeping me out of severe pain and extreme wd's - I mean, it can and probably does work. I don't think they complement each other as much as people say though. I feel like the C prevents me from appreciating my beloved H as much as I normally do. I prefer to get back to using the H when I'm coming down from the C, not while I'm still on it. I actually really dislike mixing the two, I feel like they interfere with each other but H will eliminate most of the crash of course. 


Also, it's even a painkiller somehow. I didn't think C was a known painkiller, but I live with extreme chronic pain in my spine and it helps a little bit. Not very much, nothing like H which makes it evaporate, but enough to hold me over for several hours. Completely lifts the withdrawal depression and despite all the uncomfortable physical symptoms I have always found psychological symptoms to be some of the worst of all. All of this is remarkable for something that is reputed to be a shitty, stomped on party drug mainly for people who are uneducated regarding drug use. Fishscale is the only stimulant I have any interest in at all. The doses I am using are around 10mg - I have girlfriend who has used it for 10 years anyway and she says it is very good quality. I've used it before too and hated it because it was cut trash. I guess I just felt like writing something other than "this is stomped on crap these days, not worth it, don't do it." As this is obviously way less harmful than something like Mdma or methamphetamine to the body, and way too many people do too much M these days. In my opinion this stuff is way less damaging than M but that's just my view. 


Music is vital. I've got this underworld/slightly sleezy/mysterious midnight vibe going on right now. It's chill. I think it's the coke but also the music I'm listening to (DJ Krush...Meiso) - I have it on repeat because this album just goes so well with the drug(s). Definitely improved confidence too. I feel really chilled out for a stimulant, and I get panic attacks really easily but I haven't had one at all. I do feel a little edgy but I expected that. I would never want to overdo it with this and it would be very easy to for someone not tolerant. I'd have a panic attack I think. 


It's nice having wee bits of really damn pure H and C at the same time. The C is a luxury while the H is a necessity, and I am by no means presently rich. It's tough enough to keep myself well. So I will enjoy this while it lasts, hopefully use it to lower my tolerance a bit since I really need to go from a point a day to half of one, but I never thought I'd enjoy a stimulant stronger than green tea. Especially to this extent having a high degree of depth to the nature of the high.

Fishscale typically means washed coke, namely and usually acetone washed coke to rid impurities (besides levamisimole which disolves with the coke) and it is a bit cleaner prolly 30-60%. It is a rock that glimmers like fishscales. All I ever had was touted as fishscal, in the united states, most was not but about 1/2 was actual shimmery rocks that really fuck you.


THE THING to watch out for is re-rocking after cutting with hair-spray to make it rock and shine. SMELL IT, if it smells like fingernail  polish that is the acetone which is typically a good sign in low quantities meaning a wash was done.

<!-- POST START: id=13943036 num=253 author=shmic author_id=437747 date=2017-02-08T07:16:55+0000 -->
### Post #253

**Cocaine 101. MUST READ!**


Listen guys, I'm getting annoyed with constantly looking up what effects cocaine have. You know when your off your noodle and you start researching whether or not your going to die or not, well imma put an end to all this and hope you save this thread. 


1st things 1st I'm a regular user I have been for 20+ years and I'm a business man all over Europe so I can guarantee I have tried it all.  and one things for sure nothing is 100% unless your getting it while it's just out the oven. Or you know a very good source. 


2nd of all the effects, first time users are going to use Google obviously, I still do it when I'm jamming on my own or in my offices. Trust me I have went Pete tong. 


OK the obvious one... fast heartbeat. It's a stimulant your blood pressure is gonna rise it's asking itself "what the Fuck is going on?" "DO NOT TAKE COKE REGULARLY (OR AT ALL) if you have any sort of brain, heart, vascular or lung disorder. Seriously DON'T"

Anyway stimulants increase your blood pressure. The coke you took on that binge will hit it's peak at the comedown so when your chilled you will feel it more. At the point where you start getting a headache all over but especially at the back STOP it's pressure building up between your tonsils (brain tonsils). If pressure gets stuck in there boy prepare for a nasty 10" needle I'm your spine, it's thee scariest worst painful experience of my life! If you feel your heartbeat is causing discomfort and you think your going to die... let me just put this too rest... YOUR NOT you can die off the shit you get off the street after about 5G in a night but the pure stuff. You would need to do a Scarface to die guys! 


If you start freaking out and google your symptoms it will always say your going to die. Take it from me go home or wherever you are practice your deep breaths on the way slow and steady don't be tempted to use the last bit in the bag (save it for tomorrow... you will need it ![;)](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/8.0/png/unicode/64/1f609.png).)Go home sit back hands behind your head and deep breaths, some say sitting I'm a shower stimulates your high better, but I'm my opinion it calms me down DO MOT SMOKE ANY FORM OF CANNABIS! that would just stimulate it even more and you will hit "The Fear" once you do that your on your own man. After your shower (if you do with continued deep breathing) you should feel better. But you have that come down to deal with. I have found in my personal experience that a bit off Valium from the doctors sorts you right out. It's worked with people that had anxiety attacks border personality disorder, ADHD (MYSELF) and loads more mental disorders. DEEP BREATHING IS KEY!!! if none of that works it's cause you done it on the basis of ignorance to your disorder that I mentioned at the start. If you don't have any that you know of. You should seek medical advice and make an appointment with your Dr. 


Side effects below are normal and can sometimes last for 48 hours (usually). 


Sore head 

Sick 

Instant diarrhea (first bump usually. It's because it's a stimulant. Or you just bought laxative if it's continuous) 

Euphoria

Alertness

Tingling 

Weird hand movements

Alarming heart rate 

Paranoia 

Talkative

Aggressiveness

Emotional 

Chilled 

Quiet 

Stiffness of body 

Sore eyes 

Tiredness 

Jerks 

Difficulty breathing 

Bunged nose 

Burning nose 

Numbness in face and teeth (normal!!!) 

Runny nose 

Nose bleed

Stinging nose 

Inflamed sinuses 


If you know any other side effects please add I'm sorry I can't think right now I'm noodled as we speak... oh yeah forgetfulness haha. 


OK. How to tell the good cocaine from the bad cocaine. NOT PURITY before you all start. 


First things first, if you get a guy willing to give you a tester by all means do it, ask them. The worst case is they say no and you loose or win! 


"This is my personal experience and it's never let me down" 


GOOD COCAINE: 

If your dealer gives you in rock form doesn't necessarily mean it's "pure" (I have been bumped off quite a few times by "emergency dealers") visually inspect your rock out the bag on a plate so it doesn't melt hold up to the light and check if it has a shimmer.. like a pearl or fish flake look. If it does that's GOOD it's one thing you can tick off. Next is to smell it. If you smell the rock and go "pweeew wee" that's also GOOD (petroleum smell the stinkier the better) next crush it up on the plate (or bag if your going out) and start to make a line. (I use a credit card on my first line them a razor after) cut a line with your crushed up clumps try make it room temperature. Don't put it next to something hot you will dry it out ![;)](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/8.0/png/unicode/64/1f609.png) when your cutting if it is soft to the cut and bits aren't "pinging" everywhere then that is also GOOD! (Don't mistake pinging from crunching some coke is pressed really compact and you will get the odd one or two bits flying). And last snort that bitch up !  If it goes clean up and it's a sudden rush it tastes like petrol and your off your face it's good shit!!


BAD COCAINE: 

OK so I get promised when I'm traveling "best stuff about" and it's "pure crap" luckily I have contacts now. In the event you do end up in that situation here are most of the warning signs to look out for. 


1. If it's anything but white, it's BAD 

2. No petrol smell, no go! 

3. Crumbled or pre chopped? Most definitely been cut with BAD things. 

4. What looks like dark specks I'm your baggie it's been tampered with something dodgy don't go. (Some say it's due to it being snuggled in coffee beans but if you reached stage 4 by now.. would you even risk it) 

5. If it pings while chopping it's cut with something laying about the house (baking soda, salt, paracetamol etc... you should be throwing it in the bin at this point and accept your loss) 

6. If you do end up snorting it like the fool that you are. And you get instant numbness and you end up saying (oh wow I'm off my face I'm completely numb). Get your friend to slap your face as hard as you can. Cause sorry to say it's Novocaine. (Teething powder) good coke numbs seconds after the bump. 

7. Your nose. Once you snort BAD coke it should sting after the first couple. Sometimes the 1st time (if it stings the first time and it's all of the above in "bad coke" throw it away. You do not want to have a nose if you finish it. Your nose will be on fire ! 


Your nose...


So onto the main event. The big beak! OK so first time users will experience a nose bleed. Without a doubt. I still do after 3g on a quiet night but I have a higher tolerance. Once you get that nose bleed.. "try not to use that same nostril for a while. And stick to your own straw too" it's normal. Your attacking your membrane (mines still here thankfully) 

Your nose will be major blocked after a night on the "sesh" it's your sinuses. Your Putin something up your nose that wants to attack your membrane and corrode it away. So it's getting inflamed that's why you get a blocked nose. Runny nose is normal... it's the glands trying to produce a barrier to repair what you just damaged. So constant blowing of the nose is a certainty. (This could last for days). 

Best way to handle this in my own way is to rinse your nostrils after every couple of lines warm water just sniff the water rinse it out. (IF YOU HAVE ANY OTHER EFFECTIVE TREATMENTS LET ME KNOW!!!) 


Again if you have any input on bad cocaine please let others know! 


If your reading till the end of this thread. You really shouldn't be doing drugs man. Just stop, they Fuck your life up. Don't do drugs. 


This information is based on the average person(me) 


Male 

38 

20 years doing this 

Average build 

6"3 

Travel a lot 

Business owner. 


Thanks for reading this. If you have in put please share let everyone know! 


Stay safe!

<!-- POST START: id=13947537 num=254 author=Oddie65 author_id=438286 date=2017-02-12T07:28:06+0000 -->
### Post #254

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 13947537 |
| Author | Oddie65 |
| Author ID | 438286 |
| Date | Feb 12, 2017 at 7:28 AM |
| Page | 13 |

Nice post, I'd like to add in something for inexperienced users. Cocaine in itself, even before its cut and turned into smokable forms/etc., is a dangerous drug due largely in part to its specific side effects. Vasoconstriction combined with increased heart rate and blood pressure is a perfect recipe for a heart attack, and with increased use in frequency comes greater risks because the substance destroys cardiovascular tissue on contact and this is tissue that will never fully grow back. That being said, I do love letting the white lady come visit from time to time. I don't partake the substances abuse more than once a month, with the typical schedule being once every few months when one of us finds some thats too good to pass up. 


I'd also like to add in my personal treatment for the dreaded "coke nose," and the comedown. From my few years of experience, there is no 100% cure-all that doesn't come with its own whiplash. You can use mucinex nasal spray, which uses the active ingredient "oxymetazoline" but after a day or so of use you will get a stuffy nose from actually *not *using the spray, its a habit forming substance but does work wonders for instant relief. If anything, use it before bed and it will help, and is only a few bucks at any grocery or drug store. Personally, here is what I do to deal with the dreaded comedown and "coke nose":


-No prep for the nose before indulging, and no water during the use. For me the water doesn't do much except make the drip hit really hard and I end up swallowing a good amount.

-Once I'm out and ready to head into the comedown, I boil water for tea and my sinus rinse, and take a double dose of nyquil. I don't usually have access to benzo's or even opiates, but if you do they work absolute wonders for easing the onset of sleep and putting oneself in a general feeling of comfort. It goes without saying that bud is nice to have too. Anyways, give it about an hour from your last dose, then take your benzos or opiates and start a smoke sesh if it please you. Since stimulants suppress appetites you'll likely be on an empty stomach so the onset of the medication may be quicker than usual, a good thing depending who you ask.

-Around the same time I'm ready to smoke and take any benzo's, so an hour more or less from the last dose, I go to the bathroom and do a thorough, sometimes two sinus rinses. Personally, I use the NeilMed Sinus Rise and it can be had for around $15 from a supermarket or drugstore, and that's for the starter kit that includes like 100 packets of the rinse solution along with everything else you need. The procedure is a bit awkward at first but I'm so happy I read a post from another member on here suggesting a sinus rinse. It makes a night and day difference with the intensity and recovery of coke nose, including easing a little bit of the burning once the anesthetic properties of blow wear off. 

-Once sleep is finally ready to take hold of me, if my nose is clogging up I use the mucinex spray before bed only, and only do one spray in each nostril. This keeps me comfortable long enough to go to sleep, but sometimes this isn't necessary. In the morning, my secret weapon is nasacort. Its an intranasal glucocorticoid, and is not habit forming like the oxymetazoline. It takes about an hour to an hour and a half to kick in, and has helped me recover after I went on multiple-day binges. The nasacort is rather expensive at $15-20 but lasts a while and IMO/IME is worth the price for its role is recovering from a coke binge. 


One last tip, is to only buy as much as you want to do in that one sitting/session/binge because it has been my experience and pretty much that of everyone I know who's messed with blow, that there is no moderating the stuff in terms of saving it for another time or weekend. I used to stock up when I found really fire stuff thinking I'd save it for a rainy day or something, only to find myself up for the past 24 hours working on killing a whole ball of absolute flame to myself.

<!-- POST END: id=13947537 -->

**Take with a grain of...salt?**


All very good points. I just want to add a different aspect about the mind. 


Because of my location I have found some pretty good stuff. BUT! It has taken time and a lot of trial and error. As well as learning what is good coke, and what is bad coke. Which only comes from living! I don't partake as much as I used to (growing up is a rad/daunting thing) but when I do, I know who to call and it is never a disappointment...consistent. Please please please don't do bad cocaine. What a waste of money, emotions, and time. 


However when you find your secret squirrel stash...I say this 


In my opinion it's all about your mindset. If you have a semi deep understanding of what cocaine IS and what it "represents" grasp that it's  supposed to be FUN! (Cocaines history is very interesting) but...VIBES! great talks and interactions with strangers of friends!! I would go as far to say share the fuckin stuff. Nowadays I don't even trip about it. I know I'm going to do my toots, get euphoric, talk talk talk, smoke ciggies, and have a grand ol time. But thats only because i have come to realize it has the depth of a kiddie pool compared to other substances. And I mean that in the utmost respect to all the users. Compared to say LSD, coke doesn't do much for the conscious expansion of your MinD. But boy is it a fucking barn burner. 


Anyway what I'm trying to say (I think) is don't covet thy blow. UNDERSTAND that there is never enough. Don't put the coke onto a pedastool where it doesn't belong. Share good times with your friends and maybe a couple skanky vulchers. Fuck it. For when you understand that there is much more than huddling in a bathroom bickering of who pitched on what or squawking about line size, there's so much FUN KoOky times in it! Share, love, and don't be a butthole about it.

<!-- POST START: id=14083218 num=280 author=Ignio author_id=355526 date=2017-07-10T11:46:15+0100 -->
### Post #280

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 14083218 |
| Author | Ignio |

> [shmic said:](https://www.bluelight.org/community/goto/post?id=13943036)
> 
> 
> 
> 			OK. How to tell the good cocaine from the bad cocaine. NOT PURITY before you all start. 
> 
> 
> 
> First things first, if you get a guy willing to give you a tester by all means do it, ask them. The worst case is they say no and you loose or win! 
> 
> 
> 
> GOOD COCAINE: 
> 
> If your dealer gives you in rock form doesn't necessarily mean it's "pure" (I have been bumped off quite a few times by "emergency dealers") visually inspect your rock out the bag on a plate so it doesn't melt **hold up to the light and check if it has a shimmer.. like a pearl or fish flake look. If it does that's GOOD it's one thing you can tick off. ****Next is to smell it. If you smell the rock and go "pweeew wee" that's also GOOD (petroleum smell the stinkier the better)** next crush it up on the plate (or bag if your going out) and start to make a line. (I use a credit card on my first line them a razor after) cut a line with your crushed up clumps try make it room temperature. Don't put it next to something hot you will dry it out ![;)](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/8.0/png/unicode/64/1f609.png) when your cutting if it is soft to the cut and bits aren't "pinging" everywhere then that is also GOOD! (Don't mistake pinging from crunching some coke is pressed really compact and you will get the odd one or two bits flying). And last snort that bitch up !  If it goes clean up and it's a sudden rush it tastes like petrol and your off your face it's good shit!!
> 
> 
> 
> BAD COCAINE: 
> 
> OK so I get promised when I'm traveling "best stuff about" and it's "pure crap" luckily I have contacts now. In the event you do end up in that situation here are most of the warning signs to look out for. 
> 
> 
> 
> 1. If it's anything but white, it's BAD 
> 
> **2. No petrol smell, no go! 
> 
> 3. Crumbled or pre chopped? Most definitely been cut with BAD things. **
> 
> 4. What looks like dark specks I'm your baggie it's been tampered with something dodgy don't go. (Some say it's due to it being snuggled in coffee beans but if you reached stage 4 by now.. would you even risk it) 
> 
> 5. If it pings while chopping it's cut with something laying about the house (baking soda, salt, paracetamol etc... you should be throwing it in the bin at this point and accept your loss) 
> 
> 6. If you do end up snorting it like the fool that you are. And you get instant numbness and you end up saying (oh wow I'm off my face I'm completely numb). Get your friend to slap your face as hard as you can. Cause sorry to say it's Novocaine. (Teething powder) good coke numbs seconds after the bump. 
> 
> 7. Your nose. Once you snort BAD coke it should sting after the first couple. Sometimes the 1st time (if it stings the first time and it's all of the above in "bad coke" throw it away. You do not want to have a nose if you finish it. Your nose will be on fire ! 
> 
> 
> 
> Your nose...
> 
> 
> 
> So onto the main event. The big beak! OK so first time users will experience a nose bleed. Without a doubt. I still do after 3g on a quiet night but I have a higher tolerance. Once you get that nose bleed.. "try not to use that same nostril for a while. And stick to your own straw too" it's normal. Your attacking your membrane (mines still here thankfully) 
> 
> Your nose will be major blocked after a night on the "sesh" it's your sinuses. Your Putin something up your nose that wants to attack your membrane and corrode it away. So it's getting inflamed that's why you get a blocked nose. Runny nose is normal... it's the glands trying to produce a barrier to repair what you just damaged. So constant blowing of the nose is a certainty. (This could last for days). 
> 
> Best way to handle this in my own way is to rinse your nostrils after every couple of lines warm water just sniff the water rinse it out. (IF YOU HAVE ANY OTHER EFFECTIVE TREATMENTS LET ME KNOW!!!) 
> 
> 
> 
> Again if you have any input on bad cocaine please let others know! 
> 
> 
> 
> If your reading till the end of this thread. You really shouldn't be doing drugs man. Just stop, they Fuck your life up. Don't do drugs. 
> 
> 
> 
> This information is based on the average person(me)
> 		
> Click to expand...
> — shmic said:


The shimmer of shinning fish scale cocaine can be repliaced by a number of means requiring no more than house hold products. For instance, hair spray.


The petroleum smell can actually come from a numbr of sources. I Europe it most likely comes from the big pressing machines (I don't know their real name), which distributers in the Netherlands use to press the coke back into 1 kg bricks after they have diluted it and are ready to distribute the former 90% columbian cocaine.

I guess the same is true in the US. Whether it happens in Mexico or the US I don't know. The point is that the smell of petroleum cannot be used as an indicator of good coke as it can come from a number of sources.


Regarding your bad list indicators, the same goes for petroleum. And I don't know what you mean with "pre-chopped" but if you mean that the cocaine do not come in rocks but as powder, and that this is a indicator that is is bad cocaine, your are wrong. People receiveing 1 kg will get bricks. If you order 500g you will get half a brick, if you order 250g you till get 1/4 of a brick. But lets say you order 250g from a source who have a lab test proving at 90% purty (that is with levamisol) or even better 95-99% purity (that is without levamisol) and you want it send by mail. Letters are by far the most secure method of shipment wereas packages involve more risk. So you get him to chop it into fine powder in order for it to be contained in a flat letter. The same goes for the ones using humans to transfer cocaine, they cannot exactly swallow a 250g 1/4 brick or shove it up their ass. But sorry if I misundestand you.


Pure cocaine will not "block" your nose no matter how much you take. Pure cocain will dissolve completely thus only leaving you with a running nose. When I think about it, this might actually be one of the most basic indicators of the purity of your cocaine. High purity no stopped nose, despite from dried blood. Bad cocaine will make it impossible to breath through your nose after a certain amount.


One way to get cocaine that are 90% or 99% pure are by cleaning it yourself.

Cocaine containing Levamisol (currently 70% of seized cocaine in Denmark contain levamisol) can become around 90% pure Cocaine without Levamisol can become 99% pure. There is is relatively big difference in how 99% purity cocaine looks and how 90% purity looks. 99% purity truely looks like snow crystals. But as it get pressed or cut up into lines it will start to look like regular cocaine.


![LYXrC1j.jpg](https://www.bluelight.org/community/proxy.php?image=http%3A%2F%2Fi.imgur.com%2FLYXrC1j.jpg%3F1&hash=44990f6f5da4e40a511a662c31f9e1bf)

> — toothpastedog said:


Thank you for the input. I will try to search for information there. Some countries have very detailed (and publics) statistics about seized cocaine, the amount, hoe much they seized, the purity, the drugs use to dilute it, where it originated from etc. The problem with countries or origin is that the actual cocaine can be made one place, put on a boat registered from another countries faking logs and what else the relevant authorities use the determine where the seized product came from. And this makes it very hard to achieve reliable knowledge about the differences in the cocaine produced in different countries.


But I don't know if you have experienced this in the US. Sometimes people are willing to pay more for cocaine from X country than cocaine from Y country becayse they think all kinds of things about what it means for the effects they experience when taking it. So in one month everyone demand Bolivian cocaine and other months Colombian cocaine and ofcourse the dealers suddely have "the badest fish scale diamond cocaine from Bolivia", but it is impossible for the normal street dealer to have any clue what so ever about the origin of their product. Most likely it is from Colombia as they remain the biggest producer of cocaine in the world. I don't understand this phenomenon.


You observe it on the dark web too. Dealers divide their products between Colombian and Bolivian cocaine. Though they might actually have an idea where it is from. Atleast those big enough to be selling whole or half bricks.

### Post #294

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 14144823 |
| Author | Holly.3 |

| Page | 15 |

How soon after snorting a line can you blow your nose? Then what can you do to get rid of the nasty nasal drip taste in the back your throat? I have access to some stuff that I know is cocaine because my friend bought about seven grams of fish scale and sold a little bit of it and kept a little bit and then gave me a little bit. She says it's good strong stuff. She does it a little more often than I do, a couple of times every couple of months. I did a skinny line of this three weekends ago because it's been a couple years since I've done any so I wanted to start off easy. Didn't notice any High at all, just noticed my mouth getting numb, my teeth getting them and the nasty nasal drip taste in the back of your throat. Did a bigger line last weekend still no high feeling, just the typical runny nose and numb mouth and throat and nasty nasal drip taste. Did a bigger line about 15 minutes, still no hi, just the same runny nose and numb mouth and nasal drip. I'm a triathlete so I naturally have a much lower heart rate than most people. Sitting on the couch watching TV right before taking the line my heart rate all three times taking it has been in the upper forties and then my heart rate about 10 minutes after taking it all three times has been in the low 70s. Like I said before, three weeks ago when I took the first line it was just a skinny line probably no longer than a Matchstick. The second time last weekend it was probably about the same length just a slight a bit fatter and then when I took it just now it was still probably the same length but just a little bit more fatter than last week. ( trying to be somewhat conservative with the amount of stuff I have and still try to achieve somewhat of a good high. )  right now about 15 minutes after taking the line I feel a slight good feeling. But nothing like a big rush of euphoria. I know the stuff is good because when my friend purchased the seven grams it was good fish scale.  She always does an acetone wash when she gets cocaine that she plans on selling some of. There's only one person that she sells to and like I said neither of us do cocaine on a regular basis. Back in the mid-2000s she was more into doing it and getting coked out once in awhile. Back around that same time when I was playing in bands I had access to it but never did a whole lot at one time. If I was going to do it for the night, I almost always do one line and then do two or three bumps the rest of the night and it could be a week between doses two weeks between doses or even four weeks between doses. Usually when I was doing it, it was because I was quote on quote in the band so when whoever had it was passing it around I always got a small amount. A lot of times I had stuff left over that I didn't do. Never built up a big tolerance for it. But usually got a good Buzz and good Rush when taking the first line and then the bumps we're enough to keep it going. So anyways the stuff that my friend gave me has been acetone washed and the person she sold some of it too reported back to her that it was quote unquote good stuff as usual. Anyways, other than the line I took this time giving me just a slight good feeling, no big rush or anything. I figured the other two times I took it recently the lines weren't big enough but I figured since it's the first time and doing it in a couple years that it should have been enough to get me going. I had all the effects of the cocaine except for that nice Rush that rush you get about a couple of minutes after snorting it. My friend that I got it from says that she bumped it every once in awhile when she needs a little bit of energy to get started in the day and says that it always works for her the two or three times that she buys a year she always gets from the same supplier and from what she says it's always reliable stuff. She always does and acetone wash and the same person that she always sell some of it too just wondering why I'm not getting a good high off of it. And I've always wondered how long after snorting it can you blow your nose? I've always been afraid to blow it for a fear of blowing all the cocaine back out. And is there a trick to getting rid of the nasty nasal drip taste in the back your throat?


And since I mentioned acetone washing, just how pure can cocaine be if it's been acetone washed? And can you acetone wash it more than once? Like let's say your supplier acetone washes it and then when you get it you acetone wash it not knowing it's already been washed. Well that have any effect on it?

<!-- POST START: id=14144833 num=295 author=RDP89 author_id=272977 date=2017-09-24T22:53:35+0100 -->
### Post #295

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 14144833 |
| Author | RDP89 |
| Author ID | 272977 |
| Date | Sep 24, 2017 at 10:53 PM |
| Page | 15 |

> [Lotus-tx said:](https://www.bluelight.org/community/goto/post?id=14144823)
> 
> 
> 
> 			And since I mentioned acetone washing, just how pure can cocaine be if it's been acetone washed? And can you acetone wash it more than once? Like let's say your supplier acetone washes it and then when you get it you acetone wash it not knowing it's already been washed. Well that have any effect on it?
> 		
> Click to expand...
> — Lotus-tx said:

 It could wind up very pure, but the problem is some cuts(including levamisole) aren't acetone soluble. So you can acetone wash as much as you want, and it will clean it up some, but any non-acetone soluble cuts will still be there. That's why an acetone wash and then a chloroform wash is recommended.

<!-- POST END: id=14144833 -->

<!-- POST START: id=14144861 num=297 author=RDP89 author_id=272977 date=2017-09-25T00:33:16+0100 -->
### Post #297

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 14144861 |
| Author | RDP89 |
| Author ID | 272977 |
| Date | Sep 25, 2017 at 12:33 AM |
| Page | 15 |

> [Lotus-tx said:](https://www.bluelight.org/community/goto/post?id=14144837)
> 
> 
> 
> 			Do you wash it the same way with chloroform?
> 		
> Click to expand...
> — Lotus-tx said:


No, it's actually the opposite. cocaine is soluble in chloroform at 1 gram per 12.5 mls. So you would want to discard what's left in the filter, your cocaine would be in solution in the chloroform, so you would have to dissolve that all away and be left with your cocaine crystals.

<!-- POST END: id=14144861 -->
