<!-- POST START: id=14439545 num=398 author=Holly.3 author_id=534362 date=2018-11-09T22:05:45+0000 -->
### Post #398

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 14439545 |
| Author | Holly.3 |
| Author ID | 534362 |
| Date | Nov 9, 2018 at 10:05 PM |
| Page | 20 |

So how many lines do you guys typically get out of half a gram?


A very close friend of mine who is also my supplier, over a 7-hour long night out at the Club, she told me she did 11 lines which was half a gram which she was a bit embarrassed because she very rarely does that much at one time.


I've never really thought to count how many lines I get out of half a gram or even a full gram. My friend always tells me that she does small skinny lines so her stuff will last longer and also so her sinuses won't give her trouble but yeah she was a bit embarrassed to tell me she did 11 skinny lines over a 7-hour night. She said if her two friends that she sold three grams each two weren't we as much as they were doing, she wouldn't have done the amount she did.


It's been probably three or more years since the last time I went through half a gram over a long night.


My lines are 2 and 1/2 inches long which is the length of the razor blade. Pretty skinny at both ends and then it gets a little thicker in the middle. I wouldn't say that my lines are skinny and I would definitely not say there fat. I always consider them on the lighter side of a medium-sized line if a two and a half inch line can be considered medium compared to the length of a credit card.  I just I got 3 grams from my friend yesterday. I guess I should have kept track of how many lines I get out of that half a gram over the next week and a half, two weeks or so for a better comparison before posting this. Oh well


One more question, when I first started dabbling with cocaine in my early twenties, I quickly came to the conclusion that a regular size Stanley box cutter blade a, 2 and 1/2 inches in length works a thousand times better when chopping your line in a powder compared to a credit card. I know a lot of people use credit cards and make their lines as long as the credit card. I try to never use a credit card if I don't have to. So pretty much my lines have always been 2 and 1/2 inches long. I'm not sure if that would be considered a short line or a pretty average, or if using a credit card is more of the standard. I just prefer the blade because they chops the lump or the flakes into a really nice fine powder.


I'm assuming that 11 small skinny lines ( which she said it came out to half a gram) over a 7 hour night would be considered more of a lighter usage compared to if she did the 11 lines in a four or five hour period.

> 
> 			Hey victornc, in your 1st reply you mentioned 2 units of water. How much is 2 units. The syringes I have are 1ml. And I admit (like you did) that I caved & tried it the night we 1st chatted. I used a very small amount; like the amount I would lay out for 1 line. Didn't get a huge rush or bells but could tell I did it. It was rather mild but that's good. I may've unknowingly done way more if I hadn't read your reply. Anyway, I'm out of C right now buy might recoup soon. Just curious about the question of what is 2 units? Thanks.
> 		
> Click to expand...
> — TexUSA said:


On an average 1ml syringe you will notice numbers rising up to the top from 0-100. Those are the units. There are 100units per 

1cc/1ml. 

2 units would be to the very first line that is marked on the syringe, so its 2/100ml. That amount of water won't dissolve anything. He probably meant 20 units. which is just about 1/5 of the way up the barrel. Most of the needles I have seen have the units marked in increments of 10. 

I STRONGLY encourage you to read up on IV usage and safety if your are going to do this. You dont sound all to knowledgeable on the subject and that is important if you are insistent on using this ROA. ESPECIALLY with coke. 

This drug is not for the unseasoned user when IV'd. Be careful.

I've been checking out the internet and looking at different Forums on the topic of how many lines do you get out of a gram?


A lot of these guys are bragging if they can get two or three lines out of a gram and then others say they can get 6 to 8 lines.


I'm just an occasional, just for fun user so I can get quite a few more lines then most people. Over the course of the past week I was able to get 35 key bumps out of half a gram. 4 key bumps visually equals a normal line up for me. I guess if you do the math, it comes out to an average of about 8 lines per half a gram. So that being said, I should normally average about 16 lines plus or minus a line out of a gram.


My girlfriend who was also an occasional, just for fun or went out celebrating with friends kind of a user. About a month ago she went through half a gram over 7 hours while out at the clubs with some friends. She rarely ever does that much in one night. Anyways, she was able to get 11 small skinny lines out of half a gram. Which would come out to about 22 lines plus or minus a line per gram


Neither of us are newbies or beginners. They both have over 12 years of experience with cocaine, we're just not heavy users at any given time.


How many lines do you guys normally get out of a gram? On average?

<!-- POST END: id=14444274 -->

A lot of people like to brag about how big they make their lines. In reality, the size of those huge lines would kill them 3x over with pure coke. 

They are most likely getting very poor quality cocaine which is nothing to brag about. 

If you can do small lines and feel good from them and you're not a novice, chances are you have better product than them.

**cocaine- unanswered questions- overrated?**


So I tried cocaine the other night got around 2 grams went at it alone with some drinks.  The high was good, but definitely not worth the comedown that shit sucked.  Over the course of the night I tried managing both responsibly haha did maybe .5-1g of it before I forced myself to stop in a period of 5 hours, had maybe 5 standard beers along with it.  Renounced to me later while doing research I guess cocaine interacts with ethanol to produce a more toxic drug in your bloodstream that makes the comedown worse and the high last longer.  Could not get to sleep for the life of me, 6 hours after my last line in pretty shitty depression before I slept for a couple hours and went to class.  Oh yeah, I was pounding water too and made myself eat a little halfway through the comedown.  Very jittery, not worth the high at all.  I heard taking some kind of opiate when in the comedown period works but, I did not have any opiates or depressants in that matter besides alcohol and I didn't like the thought of mixing alcohol and cocaine let alone adding in another drug.  I have a little more than half of it left and would like some suggestions on how to use it and not have a shitty shitty time.  Probably gonna take it during the day so i can sleep later and not mix it with alcohol and take it in less quantity and longer periods of abstinence.  What do you guys think would that help?  I want to do cocaine and not fuck myself up, too late for that anyways but I would rather have a good time.  Why is this drug so popular it just seems like a instant gratification with greater consequences compared to other stuff out there.

Coacaine used to be of a lot higher purity years ago. While I personally hate coke, it is one of the most euphoric substances out their.  People including myself have endured the horrible pain of drastic spikes in heart rate/ BP ,panic, and severe palpitations to get that rush.

It now very heavily cut and the feeling is hardly the same. 

Much of what is sold now are other chemicals that when combined  walk, talk, and act like cocaine. 

Very poor quality product disguised as top notch. Like Epiphone and Gibson hahaha

<!-- POST START: id=14445912 num=411 author=Holly.3 author_id=534362 date=2018-11-23T02:32:57+0000 -->
### Post #411

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 14445912 |
| Author | Holly.3 |
| Author ID | 534362 |
| Date | Nov 23, 2018 at 2:32 AM |
| Page | 21 |

I'm fortunate enough that a very close friend of mine who I get my stuff from gets her stuff from two different people. She has a third person but that's She has a third person but she only uses him for emergencies when the other two can't pull through which is not very often.


The lady is a player my friend started using back in late May who is recommended by my friend's boyfriend she knows. The lawyer guy told my friend that this lady supplier always has very high quality fish scale, pearlescent, shimmery, flaky stuff. The after scout people always talk about. My friend usually buys and quantities of 7 grams or 14 grams and then we'll keep a grandpa for herself and then sell the rest at a minimum of 3 grams. Everything she has gotten from this lady supplier has been the classic fish scale that everybody talks about. I am fortunate enough to have access where I can send a sample off to get lab tested. Everything I have sent off to get tested has been between 89% and 96% pure.


Of course with stuff that good, a little bit goes a longer way. But even with that stuff, size of my coupons are the same as I would normally do. I always find that two or three key bumps at a time goes up a further distance then doing a line at a time.


I have done on a very rare occasion a full half gram over the course of eight or nine hours. A little here and a little there. Other than the loss of appetite and not being sleepy. There is really not much of a come down. Of course, after you do that much cocaine even if it's a little each time, when you do have a gram in that amount of time regardless the quality, at some point your nose is going to start to burn and will usually burn for a couple hours once you're done for the night. But the harsh come down everybody talks about, I rarely experience that with stuff that is as good as what my friend gets from this lady supplier. 


With that being said, even though I'm just more of an occasional, "just for fun" type of user. Or if I'm going out on the rare occasion to celebrate with a few friends. I'm just as content doing a couple of bumps every week or two as I am doing 4 lines over a 6-hour night. Like I said earlier, there are the rare occasions 2 or 3 times throughout the year where I'm at with friends and over the course of a long night May do half a gram. Even though nowadays, it's easy for a gram to last me a month if not longer, I'm definitely not a newbie to using cocaine. Back in my early to Mid twenties there were times when I would go through half a gram over a long night once or twice over the course of two or three months. And during that time, there times when over the course of 24 hours I would do a full gram. But nowadays it's more just two or three pumps every couple of weeks or if I'm going out with a few friends or celebrating with friends. So I have a lot of experience with cocaine just not a regular or heavy user.


With that being said I know for a fact I've come across cocaine that has been properly acetone washed many times over the years. There's been times where I've been told it's then acetone washed and is of high quality. More times than not the stuff proved to be very decent, but I was never able to 100% prove it was actually acetone washed. I have never acetone washed cocaine and I've never seen it being properly done.


Of course when you acetone wash product, you're getting rid of 95% (if not higher) of all the crap cuts that have been put in bye 75, 80% of everyone who has touched it along the way until it gets in your hands. So yeah, it's pretty safe to say that acetone washing your cocaine is the best way 2 get your cocaine back to as pure as it's more than likely going to be until the next person starts cutting it again. So yeah properly acetone washed cocaine Purity is going to be a very high.


I've tried to do a lot of research and find out a lot of information about acetone washing your cocaine. Of course there's been post on here that are very detailed and the process from A to Z how you should go about washing your product. I've never heard or seen in pictures and of course what you see on YouTube you got to take with a grain of salt, but I've never seen what the final product should look like once it's been washed and dried.


After washing and drying your cocaine, what should the final product look like once everything is complete? What I'm trying to find out is, if you have the classic definition of fish scale, shimmery, pearlescent, very flaky and a tad bit sticky, when you have a lump of it you can take a razor blade and Flake off as much as you need without it crumbling or crushing into a powder, even the flakes are nice and shimmery and pearlescent looking. When you have that kind of fish scale cocaine, at some point could it have been acetone washed to get it back up to a much more pure state or is the fish scale that I'm getting and having samples tested with results of a very high-purity, is that cocaine that has some out slipped through the cracks and has been cut the crap and back?


Can cocaine that has been acetone washed and dried properly be altered to have a textbook fish scale look with the pearlescent shimmery look and the weighted flakes instead of crumbles without altering the purity of it?

<!-- POST END: id=14445912 -->

> — Victornc said:

Hey Victornc and also Mr.Deeds,

Have made more than 1 buy since my last post.  I had to put some Harm Reduction on myself when it came to buying a scale or not.  I know you said I probably could start with 50mg maybe.  My hesitation was that I'm 52yrs old, disabled, with Hypertension and I knew that if I had a scale in front of me, I would most likely bang 50mg.  But I wanted to know how much was the li'l bit that I had already done and asked myself if I really wanted to intensify that startling rush which I was already familiar with and run the risk of something health related happening.  So I did some research online and discovered that 1 of my Dilaudid 8mg tablets is = to 15mg in weight.  Well, since I only bang 1/2 a pill (4mg) at a time then I knew just how much coke would be = what I see in the spoon when I bang Dilaudid which is 7.5mg.  I was floored!  The 7.5mg that I already did would be, okay to repeat safely but not much more that.  I can't even imagine what I would've experienced if I had banged 50mg of coke.  Y'all are the ones that instilled in me that sense of HR and safety which led to my positive decision to not tempt myself to do something that I shouldn't be doing.  Yo know, my favorite movie is The Matrix and there's a scene in it which the Oracle talks to Neo.  There was a sign above her door in Latin.  She told him it means "Know Thyself".  Thank you Victornc and Mr.Deeds.  So now, I've been banging the coke almost every time I bang Dilaudid; "together"!  Yeah!  I mean, the excellent Dilaudid rush I get when I bang it is great but it lingers for about a minute and then dissipates.  So, this ROA mixture kind of intensifies the Dilaudid rush and helps it linger for awhile.  Sometimes, I just bang the coke by itself but I know that I'm doing 10mg or less.  In fact, halfway through this post I stopped, went and banged some coke by itself and came right back to finish typing this out.  I have a li'l tinnitus going on and my hearing sounds a tad muffled but it's all good.  For anyone reading this that are considering this ROA; stop!  I have a high Dilaudid tolerance since I've been on it many years for my chronic spinal pain.  And, if you're dead set on banging coke by itself, I would advise against it.  I've made 2 3.5g (=7g) buys since Thanksgiving.  It's not only costly but it's dangerous.  Mr.Deeds said too me "This drug is not for the unseasoned user when IV'd. Be careful.".  If your dead set on doing it though, please do you're due diligence in researching it well on BL and don't be afraid to ask questions.  We're on here for Harm Reduction purposes not for story-telling.   ~TexUSA

No, your dilaudid pill contains 15mg of dilaudid as well as additional fillers and binders. The pill * does not* weigh 15mg, it weighs a lot more than that because of those extra fillers and binders. This is a common misconception.

> 			No, your dilaudid pill contains 15mg of dilaudid as well as additional fillers and binders. The pill * does not* weigh 15mg, it weighs a lot more than that because of those extra fillers and binders. This is a common misconception.
> 		
> Click to expand...
> — MDPV_Psychosis said:

I disagree. Did much research. One 8mg Dilaudid tablet does not contain 15mg of Dilaudid. I know it contains fillers and binders but that does not mean it has almost twice the Dilaudid than what is stated in the drug manufacturers and the FDA's data sheets. My research was based on "volume weight" of one tablet and 15mg was always the answer. I'm done w/this conversation.

Hey, no worries. Check out this website for a point of reference:


[https://www.bluebulbprojects.com/measureofthings/](https://www.bluebulbprojects.com/measureofthings/)


According to them the average long grain of rice weighs about 29mg, so 15mg is about half the weight of a single grain. 


Those pills would have to be tiny if they weighed only 15mg. Manufacturers always bulk up pills so that they are easier to handle (not drop and loose forever in the carpet, etc). At 15mg it would be like a microdot, not a pill.

<!-- POST START: id=14451421 num=429 author=Sertürner author_id=485834 date=2018-12-05T02:48:29+0000 -->
### Post #429

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 14451421 |
| Author | Sertürner |
| Author ID | 485834 |
| Date | Dec 5, 2018 at 2:48 AM |
| Page | 22 |

I was very unhealthy with my IV coke use and would dose anywhere from 10-30min apart. I would suggest to wait until you are feeling somewhat "baseline" again. By this I mean no more tremors, dizziness, fast heart rate, palpitations, ect. 1-2hrs in between shots seems pretty reasonable to me as long as you know your body can handle more. What you dont want to do is slam another shot because you're fiending but in the back of your mind your body is telling you "I'm not really ready for more yet". This mentality is dangerous, and yet very common with IV coke. Dont let the urge to redose overpower what your body is able to handle.

<!-- POST END: id=14451421 -->

<!-- POST START: id=14457476 num=432 author=fifo_thekid author_id=381607 date=2018-12-16T18:19:50+0000 -->
### Post #432

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 14457476 |
| Author | fifo_thekid |
| Author ID | 381607 |
| Date | Dec 16, 2018 at 6:19 PM |
| Page | 22 |

**5% Cocaine + 15% Caffeine and the Rest is Unknown The Hard Truth About Brazilian Coke**


This is based on an interview I made with a guy I knew on Skype who lives on Rio de Janeiro. Let's call him Rodrigo. The story goes like this...


Rodrigo is a very curious guy who always looks for the truth. He is kind of perfectionist and would always like to get "the real thing". He has the knowledge and money to experiment and this led him to these conclusions that I'm pretty sure you would never see in any other place.

Our friend did not try cocaine in other countries. He was mostly confined to Rio's coke. Rio has hundreds and hundreds of favelas (shanty towns) completely controlled by criminal factions. They usually have kiosks where you can buy weed, coke and may be some other drugs. Our friend experimented with cocaine from at least 20 favelas, and he'd always notice the same thing: all the coke here is orangish and has a texture very very different from what he would see online. It looks more like powdered milk, and it has absolutely no shine to it. Still, there is a huge variety of color tones, textures, highs and side-effects between cocaine purchased from different favelas. After looking for the best available yellow coke for several years, he settled on a wholesaler which is consistently considered the best dealer in Rio. The coke comes as a big rock which looks like it has been cut from the brick, damp with a strong smell of acetone and a little bit sticky. The high is "good" and you don't particularly feel bad after taking it.

Now since he bought it for a very very low price, he thought that he would be able to experiment with that big quantity that he has. He started with anhydrous acetone wash, which almost didn't reduce the quantity. The a chloroform wash, which reduced the quantity to 70% and gave a completely different product! Now it's more granular, light yellow and the high is more subtle. It also does not clog the nose. Good news right? Now read on!

Being a curious guy, he wanted that "fish-scale" he'd always see on the Internet. He brought ammonium and muriatic and started the recrystallization process on the coke already cleaned with chloroform. First step was dissolving the coke in water and....IT DIDN'T DISSOLVE!!!! I mean, almost nothing dissolved!!! The water was full of white flakes that didn't dissolve neither with stirring nor with heating. Adding ammonium did not make any difference! He then dried the coke and put it on an aluminum foil and heated it, and it evaporated quickly! I know what you are thinking: it's cocaine base/crack. But no, it isn't. Simply because it does not dissolve in anhydrous acetone.

So..what's next?

The guy started looking online for laboratories and he found Energy Control. He sent them a 100mgs sample of uncleaned coke and after waiting for a month lo and behold: 5% coke + 15% caffeine and the rest is unknown!!!!!!!!!

So all these years has was only taking this crap? A tiny bit of coke with a mixture of caffeine and medicines?!!!

This reminded me of a conversation I had on some forum a couple months ago with a guy that allegedly knows the cartels in the Paraguay, and they told him that they prefer sending coke to the US and Europe due to the huge difference in exchange rate and purchasing power. I mean think about it: it is sold here for 10% of the US/European price.

The last thing I heard from him was that he could get in touch with a dealer (not related at all to favelas). This guy allegedly sells to foreigners and artists exclusively. It was 4 times the price of the favela coke and it looks, tastes and feels completely different from anything he has seen. It looks EXACTLY like fish scale cocaine that he sees online. However, the taste is just too bitter and it's too "ampy". He thinks that it is much much purer than that favela shit but it is almost definitely mixed with amphetamines. Now he's thinking of sending a sample to Energy Control of this "fish-scale" next months...

<!-- POST END: id=14457476 -->

<!-- POST START: id=14463676 num=435 author=Fractality author_id=320552 date=2018-12-29T07:42:57+0000 -->
### Post #435

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 14463676 |

| Date | Dec 29, 2018 at 7:42 AM |
| Page | 22 |

I would appreciate feedback on my outline for an "ultimate" wash/purification technique. Cuts do vary based on location, but this is designed to cover the most common ones for me.


1. **Ethanol/isopropyl alcohol recrystallization**

-Dissolve 1 to 2 grams of product in shot glass with 200 proof ethanol or 99%/salted isopropyl alcohol

-Filter to remove insoluble impurities

-Evaporate solution on teflon pan or glass dish


2. **Hexane extraction**

-Create freebase using typical method

-Remove water and let base dry overnight

-Mix freebase with heated to 75 degree celsius 95% anhydrous hexane

-Let it cool then add water in a sep funnel and shake until two layers are created

-Discard water layer. Repeat previous step 1-3 times

-Evaporate hexane


Now, either consume the base orally (if you have an aversion to smoking base) or turn it into HCL. Anyone have suggestions for how to turn it back into HCL? I'm getting conflicting info whether or not putting the base in a very small amount of distilled water, then adding muriatic/hydrochloric acid dropwise until base disappears, then evaporating that solution works.

<!-- POST END: id=14463676 -->

> — Madrus said:


Everyone is different but cocaine shouldn't make you nauseas to the point where you need to ask how to deal with the nausea, at least in my experience. I used to experience some nausea if I took a big hit of crack, but it would dissipate very quickly. If you are experiencing a lot of nausea I'd say that's a sign you're doing too much. Vision problems are also a sign you are doing too much.

Makes sense. Via injecting it goes like this: vein -> right part of the heart -> lung -> left part of the heart -> brain

By smoking it you skip the vein -> right part of the heart part, which can lead to a faster onset

Yeah I kind of figured nobody would be able to answer it. Was just more curious as to what the top five or so most common Cuts were. Kind of along the lines of these are the cuts that more than likely expect Orbitz that are in a couple of grams you buy on a regular basis. I know lidocaine, benzocaine, procaine are commonly used. Laxatives are commonly used, amphetamines are commonly used. Fentanyl is getting to be quite popular but I haven't read any studies that determine just how often it's being used. Is it in 20% of the cocaine you're doing or is it more than likely in 80% of the cocaine you're doing.


More of a curiosity question. Kind of like X Y and Z cuts are most commonly used and more than likely that 1/2 gram I did New Year's Eve was cut with it. I often wonder when I buy a couple of grams what Cuts I'm more than likely taking on a normal basis versus other cuts that are less commonly used.


My friend that I get my stuff from has a supplier she uses from time to time, the supplier consistently has what I would consider textbook fish, nice pearlescent and shimmery look, the lump is firm but not hard, easy to flake without crumbling. Just moist enough that it's slightly sticky to the edge of the razor blade. Slightly waxy consistency to it in the sense that it's firm but yet very easily chopped up into a nice fine fluffy powder. Noticeably starts to get a bit more sticky and slightly moist shortly after being exposed to more humid air such as storing it in your house and then taking it to your car and within a couple of minutes you can easily noticed that it's getting slightly. And a high is incredible with very minimal come down. I've done three or four easy white tests on several different samples obtained throughout the course of 2 months. The supplier claims its very good you're quality, about 93% or better. Which of course every dealer is going to claim their stuff is very pure, which I always take with a grain of salt until I've chopped up a few lines and tested a couple samples. The stuff each time I tested it with the easy white kit, the results showed the Purity on the color scale was very very dark indicating that it contain a high amount of cocaine vs cuts.  Even then I still wonder if it is let's say 90% or better, what cuts are still in it.


At one time I had access to a source that could do lab testing and determine exactly what was in your cocaine. If I knew then what I know now, I would have taken more advantage of getting it lab tested. But of course, that was back in the mid mid-2000s and for sure cocaine is cut with a lot more things today then it was back then.


Okay, well at least I tried with my question. I can find stuff on the internet but nothing that rates the cuts from most commonly used to least commonly used.


I buy in small quantities, usually less than 5 grams at a time on average and only have about 5 people that I buy for me on occasion. I don't have the means or the knowledge of how to cut cocaine nor do I find it worth cutting a gram just to get a gram and a half out of it.

Changing the subject slightly...


Why do some Steelers put duct tape around the little gram baggie before selling? I have one supplier I use as a backup. Everything you get from her as always individually backed up into those really teeny 1in by 1in gram bags. She well then put duct tape whether it's a solid color or has a pattern on it around the whole bag and even slightly above the opening and then folding the tape back onto itself, Sticky Side to Sticky Side allowing the opening of the bag to have about a quarter of an inch of duct tape above the opening but still allow you to be able to access and and reseal the bag.


I used at the supplier that's my go-to throughout the month of May June and July last year and then on and off quite regularly another two months. Her product is very consistently the textbook description of fish scale. I've even sent a couple of samples at different times to a lab what's the results coming back both times above 87% purity. I know you just her more as a backup or when somebody request the "real good stuff" 


Every time I have bought from her which requires a minimum of a 5-gram purchase, everything is always been individually packaged and those little teeny one gram size baggies. Each time I purchase it from her, the baggies have always been duct-taped. 


Is this to conceal what's on the inside so you can't see it? 

Or is that her style of calling card? (Some people use baggies with Ace of Spades or Superman or Stars printed on the baggie which allows people buying to identify the source depending on what's printed on the baggie).

She consistently has fish scale and the two times I tested it having results of very high quality. From my experiences with her, one time doing about 5 lines and taking hits off of her bong over a 3 1/2 to 4 hour time span. She doesn't come across as a mid-level dealer or she has lots of guns with armed guys by her side waiting for something to go down. She's probably a higher up low-level dealer where she can get stuff straight from Mexico but still keeping it low-key and nonchalant not making it obvious that she deals. But everything I've ever gotten from her has always been weighed and deals. But everything I've ever gotten from her has always been weighed in 1 gram increments and packaged in one gram individual baggies instead of just selling you a 5-gram lump and one of those four or five gram size baggies you get at the smoke shops.


My question is a, what's the purpose for duct taping the bags. Or is it more just her personal preference of how she wants to do it with no real specific purpose for taping the baggies

<!-- POST END: id=14488181 -->

<!-- POST START: id=14488287 num=465 author=Holly.3 author_id=534362 date=2019-02-21T09:58:02+0000 -->
### Post #465

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 14488287 |

| Page | 24 |

What household item or what object other than an actual calibrated weight weighs exactly, precisely, 1 gram? Not something that weighs approximately but something exactly one gram that I can use to check the accuracy of portable digital scale?


I picked up 3 grams from a very close trusted friend. The normal two or three gram size baggies that come 100 to a package that you can buy from any smoke shop, when empty consistently weigh on my scale .6 grams. I've never weighed an empty baggie on her scale but I assume it would have the same result. So on my scale if I weigh a gram while it's still in the baggie it should come out to 1.6 grams.


Today when I picked up 3 grams from her she was using a different baggy, slightly larger and made of slightly thinner plastic. Not sure what the baggie weighs empty. She put the three grams in the baggie on her scale and it showed 3.2 grams. I have no reason to not trust that she shorted me on my three grams. When I got home I put the baggie on my scale just out of curiosity and it showed 3.6 grams


So now I'm curious to see how accurate both the scales are. What can I use that weighs exactly precisely 1 gram so I can test the accuracy of each scale and determined if 1 scale is off and I can't be calibrated correctly then it definitely needs to be replaced.


A brand-new nickel supposedly is supposed to weigh 5 grams. Not sure how accurate that information is, and not sure is it exactly 5 grams or can it very from 4.9 to 5.1 grams

I used to have a good family friend that was a Narcotics officer for 27 years before retiring from the Houston Police Department. Back in 2007. He now lives out in California. It?s one of those knowledge things that should be passed from experienced IV user to novice users. Not to be attempted alone.

Gotta have experience taking a test sniff and waiting an hour to know the quality of your product. Not something you want to be learning via trial and error. 

IV coke is way less forgiving than IV meth IMO... the safety margins are greater for meth than coke. You can accidentally shoot .1gs more meth than intended and just suffer horrible anxiety and insomnia. Coke is not as forgiving. .1g extra could equal a seizure and or death.

<!-- POST START: id=14489462 num=469 author=klgrtrt author_id=502770 date=2019-02-23T22:33:55+0000 -->
### Post #469

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 14489462 |
| Author | klgrtrt |
| Author ID | 502770 |
| Date | Feb 23, 2019 at 10:33 PM |
| Page | 24 |

Hi there,


over the last year or so, I've started using coke on a regular basis (strictly intranasally), mostly in order to escape my chronic depression and to get myself to do some work, be it a job-related stuff or my creative outputs such as writing or music. Before that, I was sometimes using a designer drug known to me as "Charge" to achieve the same results. It honestly worked much better than coke  but also came with horrible, soul-draining comedowns (much like speed, for better or worse, does), and eventually, the source ran dry and a much less effective substance was substituted for it (the original one was flephedrone, a mephedrone derivate, the other one I don't recall but it sucked). At the same time, I gained a ridiculously easy access to coke and gradually succumbed to it, ending up using it far more regularly than anything before. The quality was not always the best (I had one other source which gave me a pretty solid point of reference regarding what good coke is about), but (probably) regardless of that, the desired effects were increasingly less reliable and the negative effects such as increased heart-rate and general physical discomfort became a common issue. 


At some point, I sought treatment and among else, started taking drug tests every week. However, due to a pretty rapid pharmacokinetics of coke, it left me with some limited opportunities to go on with using. So right now, I am treating myself to half a gram once a week, as a sort of reward for enduring the whole week being more or less functional while experiencing a severe mental suffering most of the time, despite regularly taking high doses of SSRIs and Lamotrigine + occasionally some Modafinil. The thing is, it mostly sucks. It stimulates me for a little while, but soon, it just starts to feel uncomfortable. Above all, it makes me extremely aware of my heart activity - even though my heart rate remains between 110 and 120 bpm (which I understand is still below the truly alarming numbers) and mostly regular, I just become overwhelmed by the very sensation of the heart beating and the slight yet continuous chest pain to go with it. I am pretty sure it has something to do with the effect of various cutting agents such as caffeine, lidocaine, benzocaine or levamisole, but at the same time, it feels like a sign of my body being no longer able to handle the effects of coke, possibly even having developed some kind of cardiovascular issue as a result of the regular use in the past year. It might also be psychosomatic to some degree, me getting used to carefully watch myself and eventually augmenting the symptoms such as tachycardia just by worrying about it too much. However, I usually end up taking the edge off with some wine or beer, no matter how big of a no-no it is to my liver... Such outcome is not unfamiliar to me, but currently, it has pretty much become a rule. And I find it odd in a way, since I have been now for some time sticking to a much healthier lifestyle, eating well, regularly exercising, having stopped smoking months ago etc. Which makes me ask some ludicrous questions such as - could it be that the more fit I am, the less capable I am of handling coke? Was I previously able to use it at times even daily because my body was so fucked up that it sort of accepted it as a standard contribution to its metabolism?


All in all, my question is: Regardless of the great individual variability of how all these different factors may manifest themselves, would you ascribe the undesirable effects of taking coke once a week, as described above, to the poor quality of the product or rather me having become so maladapted to the effects of coke in general? 


No matter what the answer is, it is obvious that I should just ditch the habit entirely, since it only does me harm by now. I guess I continue to pursue it because no matter how bad it may feel, it still takes my mind off my usual shit and thus offers me some kind of temporary relief...


Anyway, sorry for tl;dr, by all means, I will appreciate any sort of feedback. Thanks.

<!-- POST END: id=14489462 -->

### Post #471

More good news about Levisamole:


> Cocaine adulterant may cause brain damage; Higher levamisole content, lower brain power
> 
> 
> 
> In order to estimate the consumption of cocaine and the amount of levamisole content, the scientists analyzed hair samples of their study participants. Based on this, they examined the cognitive performance of those who had taken cocaine with a high levamisole content (more than 25% proportional to the cocaine) and those who had taken cocaine with a low levamisole content (less than 25% ), and compared the results with a control group who had not taken cocaine.
> 
> 
> 
> As expected, the cocaine users showed lower performance than non-users in all areas -- attention, working memory, long-term memory, and executive functions. However, those who had consumed cocaine that also contained a high level of levamisole showed even greater impairment in their executive functions than those who consumed cocaine with lower levels of levamisole, even though the amount of cocaine they had taken was the same.
> 		
> Click to expand...
[https://www.sciencedaily.com/releases/2018/10/181031101028.htm](https://www.sciencedaily.com/releases/2018/10/181031101028.htm)

I know you said you have a high tolerance to benzos but 150mg does seem excessive. By 100 clonidine do you mean 100 tablets, 100mgs? Clonidine is active in the .1-.3 range.

I can?t recommend you take this many sedatives. Try starting out with 30-40mg of Valium, and take a tiny bit of clonidine. What?s crucial is that you wait at least an hour to see how you respond. For God?s sake do not take all those pills at once! You can always take a little more but you can?t un-take a handful of pills. 

Just tell your husband you?re feeling anxious about something happening tomorrow and just read a book to ?try? to take your mind off it.

Please be safe and use good judgment. Taking a decent dose of Valium is one thing (so long as you don?t combine with alcohol or opiates) but taking a huge dose of clonidine is a whole other matter.

Stay safe

### Post #474

| Field | Value |

| Page | 24 |

Just had a look through this thread and am staggered at the sheer amount of misinformation offered on a harm reduction forum.


Please people - nobody can ascertain how pure / impure / identity of cuts etc etc by either looking at cocaine, smelling cocaine, touching cocaine, tasting cocaine and definitely not by reading about your cocaine! Everything can be (and often is) faked.


You want to know what's in your product? Easy - send it to Energy Control lab in Spain and for a fee they will provide a full analysis  including percentages. Alternatively send to Wedinos in UK and they will tell you what is in your product  (no percentages though) for free.


Coke is increasingly being adulterated with new RC's. Levamisole is in a LOT of cocaine (particularly so in the States) and can be devastatingly unhealthy. Very happy to say that my personal consumption of  this stuff is (hopefully) firmly behind me


Be safe(r) everyone, much love

<!-- POST END: id=14498074 -->

### Post #489

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 14694269 |
| Author | Holly.3 |
| Author ID | 534362 |
| Date | Dec 13, 2019 at 6:58 PM |
| Page | 25 |

I know the bleach test is very basic and somewhat okay primitive way to test cocaine purity


A few questions that I've only been able to find answers that were a bit vague. I have read the article in the cocaine users handbook butt was still a bit confused in regards to the answers to my questions.


First question, how should the cocaine react when coming in contact with the Bleach? The stuff that slowly floats to the bottom leaving a somewhat milky, cloudy Trail cocaine or is it the cut floating to the bottom?


If it floats to the bottom and doesn't completely dissolve, is that the cut?


Should the cocaine dissolve immediately without floating to the bottom, leaving eight slightly oily residue on the surface of the bleach?


Or, is whats slowly floating to the bottom leaving the trail, the actual cocaine?


I've had very good quality fish scale that with an EZ test kit add results of very high cocaine content that one tested with bleach, it slowly floated to the bottom leaving a trail. It also left a slightly or any residue on the surface where the actual cocaine was in contact with the Bleach. And also did not leave any residue undissolved at the bottom of the glass.


How exactly do you determine what is the cocaine and what is the cut? I assume the residue that doesn't dissolve is the cut.


What I'm unsure of is, what do you want to see? Lots of trails as it's only flows to the bottom or a minimal amount of trails? Are trails that are left behind a good indication or a bad indication?

<!-- POST START: id=15393577 num=499 author=higherconciousness author_id=178700 date=2021-12-27T01:18:59+0000 -->
### Post #499

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 15393577 |
| Author | higherconciousness |
| Author ID | 178700 |
| Date | Dec 27, 2021 at 1:18 AM |
| Page | 25 |

To be completely honest I've always found cocaine to be one of the most overrated compounds out there. It's annoyingly short duration and fleeting glimpses of pleasure or euphoria always left me with a sense of great disappointment. It would increase anxiety, leave me nervously stimulated and at times dysphoric.  I haven't done much of it throughout my life, but I figured the quality of product I used was above average. Needless to say I wasn't really interested in trying it anymore.


For whatever reason something piqued my interest to give it a last trial run. I previously had always dealt with products sourced directly from the streets. This time I procured the cocaine from a reputable online vendor.


I received it shockingly fast and then I proceeded to lay out a few lines. From what I've gathered this appeared to have all good visual characteristics of good cocaine, so I was feeling cautiously optimistic. In nervous apprehension I gently insufflated both lines.


I was expecting much, but to my surprise a relaxed and focused energy came washing over me. I wasn't left agitated and uncomfortable. My thought processes became much more fluid and my cognitive clearer with a subsequent increase in sociability. This lasted for 30-40 minutes before the disire for another redose emerged.


Even after multiple rounds I was able to retain most of these pleasant effects.  I was expecting a nasty crash, but it wasn't as bad as I had anticipated. 


I guess I never really encountered decent cocaine, but after this stuff I definitely see the appeal of it.

<!-- POST END: id=15393577 -->

Hey Guys, 


Not posted in a while, thought I'd just check the fuck in with the fellow bluelighters to share my current situation. I been messing around with coke for the past couple of years in varying amounts. Anyway, I got a plug for some really high quality yay- this shit was like butter to snort and kicked like a mule, easily the best coke I've had. Anyway, I had a week off work and studying and my girl was away visiting family so I was like why the hell not? Bought myself a ball, went through that in a few days just drinkin and gaming/chillin with some friends who bought some for themselves/surfin the interwebs/zoom callin my girl...ended up buying myself another gram and I think i finished that in a day/night. All in all I did like 4.5g in a week after not using any coke at all for probably about a month?- I've been back at work and uni for a couple of days now and my nose fucking hurts so bad + I feel like garbage haha. 


I'm not overly worried or anything, I was making sure to saline rinse and use coconut oil on my nose every night- stayed pretty good with eating and hydration + was sleeping pretty good at the time all things considered...I  spent too much money on dumb shit but eh, shit happens.


But yeah, railing lines for like 6 days really beat the shit out of me. My brain feels like it's running at about 60%, I normally go to the gym like every day and I have absolutely no motivation to exercise- I can barely concentrate on any kind of complex task and my nose absolutely wrecks + is producing some highly questionable material to say the least. 


I'm just taking it easy on myself this week, not forcing myself to do anything too challenging and eating plenty of good food. Hopefully I'll get back to normal soon and never repeat this completely ass-backwards waste of time/money lol. 


Hope everyone is doin good ![:)](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/8.0/png/unicode/64/1f642.png)

An amphetamine cut is definitely possible. 


I would think an acetone wash would remove most of the cut, but I'm not sure if it would work to remove amphetamines from cocaine, as many people do acetone washes on amphetamines to remove cuts. [@negrogesic](https://www.bluelight.org/community/members/34956/) or [@Xorkoth](https://www.bluelight.org/community/members/77889/) might have a better answer.

Good quality DN cocaine, mixed with small amt. of heroin #3 IV.

The audial distortion... the rush, it's nice. Too nice. Must not redose...

Surprisingly heart-rate remains below 70bpm while laying down. Perhaps taking ashwagandha supplement beforehand, which is allegedly calming, helps with this.

Explain something, experts:


> Cocaine significantly increased beta in frontal and central areas and enhanced alpha in frontal and temporal regions. Cocaine-induced increases in EEG beta power had a cortical distribution similar to those produced by **barbiturates** and **benzodiazepines**. As all of these drugs reduce cortical glucose metabolism, the increases in beta power may reflect a **reduction** in cortical neural activity.
> 		
> Click to expand...


![pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov](https://www.bluelight.org/community/proxy.php?image=https%3A%2F%2Fcdn.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov%2Fpubmed%2Fpersistent%2Fpubmed-meta-image-v2.jpg&hash=60139e87a9c8640158d1b284c92d97fa&return_error=1)


##### Cocaine-induced increases in EEG alpha and beta activity: evidence for reduced cortical processing - PubMed

To understand the effects of cocaine on the cerebral cortex, 14 male polydrug abusers were enrolled in a study on the effects of cocaine on the electroencephalogram (EEG). The experimental treatments were placebo, 20 mg cocaine or 40 mg cocaine i.v. administered in a double-blind, pseudorandom...


![pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov](https://www.bluelight.org/community/proxy.php?image=https%3A%2F%2Fcdn.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov%2Fcoreutils%2Fnwds%2Fimg%2Ffavicons%2Ffavicon.png&hash=38a93253fc15d6430d52f4a6d11ea7d5&return_error=1)

					pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov
				


How is it that a stimulant is associated with a **reduction **in neural activity?

How is it that the stimulant cocaine produced similar changes as seen from ***barbiturates**** and ****benzodiazepines****?*


Fill in my gap of understanding this please.

Thanks. If the alpha-blocker clonodine only affects a1 and a2 receptors then why is the pleasure part of the cocaine blocked?


---- Unrelated 2nd post ----

Beta-blocker fear is unwarranted?


![www.cmaj.ca](https://www.bluelight.org/community/proxy.php?image=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.cmaj.ca%2Fsites%2Fdefault%2Ffiles%2Fimages%2Fcmaj-social-image.jpg&hash=2dc294066feb3f9afca2e3b91d12a479&return_error=1)


##### Avoidance of β-blockers in patients who use stimulants is not supported by good evidence

KEY POINTS Physicians often hesitate to prescribe β-blocker therapy for patients who actively use stimulants, even for indications such as heart failure with reduced ejection fraction and tachyarrhythmias, worrying that potentially harmful interactions will outweigh well-established benefits.[1][1


![www.cmaj.ca](https://www.bluelight.org/community/proxy.php?image=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.cmaj.ca%2Fsites%2Fdefault%2Ffiles%2Fimages%2Ffavicon.ico&hash=11b3fee3be9cc31c9fed1e66e0091e03&return_error=1)

					www.cmaj.ca
				


> - Evidence does not support a high risk of harms from the combination of β-blockers and stimulants, and the best available evidence suggests long-term β-blockers are safe in the context of stimulant use.
> 
>

....at least my recent experience in Chattanooga, TN:  It's **hit **or** miss.**


As some of y'all know, I dabble in coke now & then. I got the urge about a week ago. On an impulsive whim (rare for me these days) I bought a gram from a source I'd never dealt with before. Mistake! It was bunk. I had no way to test it, but my educated guess is that it was 80% levamisole. After doing 4 lines, I threw the rest in the garbage can-- and believe me, I am not in the habit of trashing drugs. Of course I'll never buy anything from that person again.


So I still had a hankering for blow and yesterday a coworker said he could hook me up. I went for it and this shit is FIRE! I'm flying high and it's the reason I'm texting to y'all right now-- I just HAD to share ♥  

Here's the kicker: the good stuff was significantly *cheaper *than the bunk! Go figure.


So y'all be careful out there. Use caution and know who you're dealing with.


Love ya! Bye for now...

I actually got a gram of coke for the first time in a long time recently. At first I sampled a small amount and thought it was meh quality (likely due to some 4F-MPH that i had taken a few hours beforehand). But when I tried it again on a different day it was quite good.


Problem is, I have a pretty significant permatolerance to cocaine due past crack/freebase use, as well as very heavy MPH and MPH analog use. This, combined with the cross tolerance bestowed to me by my current adderall script (which I don't use on the same day as drugs like MPH analogs or cocaine), means that a gram of cocaine doesn't go very far these days (if cocaine cost $30 a gram I'm sure I'd buy alot more of it, but it doesnt -- unless you buy a couple ounces of it). Given the expense of cocaine it doesn't make much sense, nor do I get particularly high when snorting it. Smoking the freebase is a different story, but I'm trying to avoid that mousetrap these days. I did cook up one rock just to gauge how pure the cocaine was, which when smoked produced a far more satisfying effect than when sniffed, but I was able to control myself from cooking up more.


I like quiding coca flour as well, produces a far more usable stimulation. When I'm snorting cocaine I'm back at the chopping block within 40 minutes.

A lil late but with some high quality someone told me about hot plating it, this my first post so idk if it’s common knowledge so I’ll explain briefly jic, basically microwaving a plate that’s a nice surface to cut on and while it’s hot(maybe like gotta be bouncing it on your hands hot) cut up your yay on it and it’ll help get it more powdery by removing the moisture cause when it’s like how you said and you don’t break it properly it can leave you hurting at least in my experience. Well depends on how occasional.. IMO a few times a month is too much for a lot of reasons.  I’d say 3-6 times a year would be max safe consumption in my eyes.  Maybe I’m wrong, but tolerance alone will continue to go up (and lasts a long time) if used any more than that.


-GC

<!-- POST START: id=15679707 num=534 author=Puff author_id=561191 date=2022-11-08T02:58:54+0000 -->
### Post #534

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 15679707 |
| Author | Puff |
| Author ID | 561191 |
| Date | Nov 8, 2022 at 2:58 AM |
| Page | 27 |

is very tricky this idea of occasional, because there is the possibility of you find excuses to make this an habit.

But this is my experience: at first I used only on weekends, but I have some moments where I want to use everyday because work is hard and because I want to feel the same happiness I felt when I used for the first time (which will never happen). I'm entering on a line of addiction that started because I have this idea of "occasional use". Today I didn' t use after one week snorting 0,5 - 1 gram per day.

The best option is to avoid the best you can because cocaine will never satisfy you. Your body will always ask for more and more.

However, if you want to use and have self control, try to establish some limits. I just don't snort more than I do, because I try to occupy my mind with other thing (like study, watch a movie) before I move to the next line. I also think a lot about the money and how I could do other things beside the drugs with this money. Maybe some mental strategies could help. I'm just not so f* up like I should thanks to this mental strategy and the little self control I have..

<!-- POST END: id=15679707 -->

### Post #545

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 15688419 |
| Author | BeepBoop91 |
| Author ID | 458321 |
| Date | Nov 18, 2022 at 5:46 AM |
| Page | 28 |

Tried cocaine for the first time this week. Bought half a gram. Diced it into 4 lines.


Took 1 line, every 20 minutes. Was nice. Pleasant. That's about it. 


After the last line, about an hour later I took 20mg of valium and 50mg of seraquel. I feel relaxed, sleepy, a little headache, probably since I havent eaten and need to drink water. I can see why people get super addicted. Thankfully in Australia its too fucking expensive lol. I'd probably be happy doing half a gram, once or twice a year. Couldn't afford anymore anyway.


I'm a daily methadone user, prescribed valium for anxiety, try not to abuse it, mostly I do alright unless its a particularly shit week or whatever. Originally addicted to Tapentadol. Nasty stuff in my opinion. 


Just my little story. In case it helps anyone.

<!-- POST END: id=15688419 -->

Yep….I just finished a 6 month daily Cocaine usage. $200 for 2 grams of decent Cocaine, always oily, shimmering, just a hint of moisture (not dry, hard pressed white powder like smashing a Tylenol tablet into powder), oily to the touch and noticeable classic odour of coke, and frequently produced euphoric talkative happy upbeat mood when having a few beers. Smoking cigarettes with a few buds and blasting lines.


Daily I would snort thin medium lines here and there, in morning after Methadone 80mg, breakfast and then a Jin & ginger ale when Methadone kicks in, snort a nice line in my bedroom and head out to outdoor patio for cigarette and 2.oz Jin cocktail. Night time, same thing.


$200 / 2 grams of Cocaine would last 4 days on average …..every week, $200 for a fat little sack of moist, oily, shimmering flakes of great Yayo. 6 months…….,f@ck. Totally unsustainable and a gross waste of money


I get 120 of Methylphenidate (Ritalin) every month/time I pick up my 100 Methadone tablets (25mg each)


It’s been 3 weeks now, no Cocaine……weird at first…..flat emotions, no vigilance or drive. I have been taking Bupropion 150mg XR in morning and a mixture of Methylphenidate (Ritalin) analogs, great considering Cocaine & Ritalin are very similar in their MOA


4-Fluoro-Methylphenidate & Isopropylphenidate 


Mostly 4F-MPH and a little IPH in a jel capsule. Very tiny bumps to get a little rise in Dopamine & Norepinephrine in my CNS. The Bupropion helps too….but every other day….I smoke and reduces pleasure of nicotine

When coke is pure and you have no tolerance 0.5 – 1g is A LOT! A gram of coke as pure as it gets is enough for a night, for a few persons without tolerance. But tolerance builds up so fast that within weeks or months you end up doing amounts that would kill a person without tolerance and it ain’t hard at all to do many grams over the day/night. Only nose is the limit lol. Lungs and veins being able to take in a lot more makes for a disaster. I only smoked it and really liked it and as for I.V. advice from just about any (ab)user – not only once – is a good one. I would say even smoking it might be best skipped as most of those who don’t find cokes high impressive when snorted, usually do when smoked.

### Post #581

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 15893902 |

| Author ID | 571566 |

| Page | 30 |

I would say that depending on factors like weight of the person, age, metabolism, heart health and what not that influences resistance to side-effects and toxic-effects of coke even less could be very dangerous. I would say that even those who can handle it better than average would experience signs of overdose anywhere between 100 and 250mg snorted in one line. Whole gram effectively absorbed at once would be very terrible and certainly kill some. In reality a lot would end up as a drip and would clog up nose at least somewhat and slow absorption but would still be very dangerous.

> — new2drugs said:

Hey I am sorry this was missed.  Members that would know are too busy drinking and doing blow. (just kidding)


I grew up at a time when doing cocaine and drinking was common.  Hell even a snort of heroin at the end was in fashion before the Reagans made all drug users look like criminals.  So cocaine and heroin became the bad drugs.  But drinking was common, and the info we have today on what happens when mixed is more robust than we had back then.  I myself have used cocaine and drank, took methaqualone and used heroin to come down.


I have pondered this question for years.  If you go to South America the cocaine is great.  When I lived in Houston that great cocaine would come into the port, and most dealers I knew would keep it that way and up the price. A few times desperate dealers would cut it more too.  But in Texas and Southern California, the only places I used cocaine 40 years ago the cocaine was good. Clean, a line made you feel just super human, not edgy, at least if the amount was kept low.  Any cocaine will wire you if you do enough.


So I ponder does this good cocaine leave SA and make it to the UK, Australia, New Zealand, et... as uncut?  Would it come into a port the same as it leaves South America or does it get stepped on to high heaven all along the distance?  Can anyone guess?  I know the the closer to SA the better it was.  And I always wondered if it makes it that distance as pure or get cut all along the way?  Not that anyone would totally know, just something I pondered.

<!-- POST END: id=16145638 -->

Okay so I got 2 packs delivered today. I went a little crazy one night and got a shit load of different compounds. One pack contained a g of cocaine. I’ve been hesitant to.Use it as I took amphetamines earlier around 10 AM. It was one line of amp sulfate so I think nine hours is plenty of time to try some of this white out. 


Well on the way back from the post office I stopped at the smoke shop to get some vapes and some nitrous for my psychs. Last night, I was casually looking at binding affinities and apparently 7-OH  has a higher affinity for the mu receptors than the suboxone I’ve been on for eight years. I wanted to see if this was true, so I got a pack of six 14mg tabs. Well, it most definitely works. I just took 2 1/2 tabs and I’m nodding out. First time in eight years I’ve had these effects. Then it dawned on me that I have cocaine.


Just did a couple of bumps so let’s see how it goes. Going to start low and go from there.
